Japanese Police Rampage in Eastern Route 44

Kharbin Railway Workers' Club Ordered to Close, News from Bo Li (Khabarovsk) and Harbin: The Manchurian police are constantly destroying cultural and educational institutions on the Chinese Eastern Railway. So far, four of the Kharbin Chinese Eastern Railway workers' clubs (the largest cultural center in Manchuria, including the Harbin Railway Hall) have been closed. The Japanese and Manchurian newspapers first made preliminary provocative propaganda, falsely claiming that the railway workers' clubs were organs for various conspiracies, etc., which led to this action. On July 6, the anniversary of the Soviet Constitution, the police did not allow dramas to be performed in various clubs and dispersed the audiences gathered at the clubs. Finally, the Soviet Union's Consul-General to Manchuria, Slavutsky, made a strong application to the Manchurian side, and the order was cancelled that evening. On July 10, the same actions were repeated, the police again prohibited the clubs from performing dramas, and expelled the patrons in the summer gardens set up by the clubs. These actions have aroused public outrage among the residents of Kharbin, because the Chinese Eastern Railway clubs were originally the only cultural and recreational institutions for the railway workers and other residents of Kharbin. (18th Tass dispatch)

Chaotic Situation in the San Francisco Labor Strike

Johnson's Mediation, Success or Failure Is Uncertain 48

Anti-Red Movement Rigorously Enforced on the Pacific Coast, San Francisco, the General Strike, San Francisco has been Blockaded for Three Days, and Today It Is Gradually Showing a Trend of Relaxation. However, Observers Still Dare Not Predict Tonight Whether Today's Developments Will Lead to the Failure of Union Workers, Will Director Johnson of the Rehabilitation Administration Force a Fair Solution, or Will the Union Try Again? Shipping Companies Believe That the Shipping Strike Has Failed, Which Can Be Confirmed in Several Ways, But the Dockworkers' Leaders Still Insist and Deny That the Strike Has Failed. Although Mayor Rossi Has Requested the Withdrawal of the San Francisco Garrison, Governor Merriman Is Still Increasing Troops and Entering the Port. Merriman Claims That 1,200 Communists Are Currently Inciting the Strike in the Port Area and Are Brewing a Rebellion in the Surrounding Area, With the Ultimate Goal of Overthrowing the California Government. However, the Union Claims That It Took Rapid Action Yesterday to Purge Communist Elements Within the Union and Prohibit Violence. It Is Heard That 40 Communists Have Been Arrested and Imprisoned in the Putnam Area. The Anti-Red Movement Is Now Very Radical. Anti-Red Elements Have Conducted Night Raids Repeatedly Along the West Coast, Dragging Hundreds of People Out of Their Beds Each Time, But Only a Small Number of Anti-Communists. Governor Merriman Ordered an Additional Garrison to Be Stationed in O'Claire to Suppress the Riots. (18th National Telegraph)

San Francisco Dockworkers' Leader Harry Bridges, an Australian, Claimed Today That the General Strike Is Over, But the Dockworkers Have Not Failed. He Also Said That the Strike Committee's Permission for Gasoline Stations and Restaurants and Meat to Resume Full Operations Weakened the Goal of the General Strike. General Johnson, Director of the National Rehabilitation Administration, Claimed Today That If the Strike Is Completely Stopped, He Can Recommend Withdrawing the National Guard. (19th Reuters dispatch)

San Francisco Dockworkers' Leader Harry Bridges, an Australian, Now Denies That He Ever Said That the General Strike Is Over, But Public Utilities Are Gradually Recovering, and Fresh Food Supplies Are Uninterrupted. It Can Be Seen That Although the General Strike Is Not Over, It Is Gradually Weakening. (19th Reuters dispatch)

The San Francisco General Strike Committee Met Here Today and Debated Fiercely. The Motion Proposed by Radical Bridges, Advocating Reconsidering the Arbitration Case Passed by the Committee Yesterday, Was Rejected by the Majority Twice. Bridges' Proposal Aims to Extend the General Strike. (19th Reuters dispatch)

The Strike's Proposal to Accept Arbitration Is Clearly Directed at Shipowners and Extremists. Shipowners Have Agreed to Submit Various Disputes to Arbitration and Agreed to Jointly Manage the Dock Employment Management Office, But the Dockworkers, Led by Australian Harry Bridges, Now Reject This Method, Believing That Shipping Companies Will Still Dominate. The Dockworkers Agreed to Submit the Matter of Submission to Arbitration to a Public Vote, But Stipulated That Shipowners Must Recognize the Statements of the Strikers and That They Should Also Be Resolved Through Mediation. Otherwise, the Submission to Arbitration Cannot Be Considered Valid. Now That Negotiations Aimed at Resolution Have Begun, the People of San Francisco Are Pleased. (18th Reuters dispatch)

The San Francisco Labor Dispute Mediation Committee Advocated Today That the Strike Be Stopped Immediately and That All Disputes Be Submitted to Arbitration, and Claimed That the Dock Employers Had Agreed to Accept Arbitration. (18th Reuters dispatch) The Panic at the Beginning of the San Francisco Strike Has Now Almost Disappeared. Shipowners Met This Afternoon to Consider the Strike Committee's Proposal to Accept Arbitration for Resolution. (19th Reuters dispatch)

French Mega-Fraud Case

Tiddio's Testimony 58

Asserting That Stavisky Should Bear All Responsibility　　Fearing It Will Cause Political Repercussions (Paris) Former Prime Minister and current Minister without Portfolio Tiddio testified before the Stavisky case parliamentary investigation committee, saying that at the beginning of the Stavisky case, some people in the authorities knew the details very well, but deliberately pretended not to know, these people made propaganda, intending to blame others, and thus slandered him (Tiddio), and there were check stubs (that is, the ticket stubs of Stavisky issuing checks to the political world) that were tampered with, but experts had stated that the handwriting of the check stubs was unrecognizable and proved that there must be tampering. Although he repeatedly requested to testify in court to explain the whole story, he was not summoned until today. Tiddio then said that he did not know Stavisky until January 1933, when he learned that the Volonté newspaper was controlled by him. Tiddio continued to say that the 17 members of parliament involved in the Stavisky case were not his (Tiddio's) friends. Tiddio also said that from the beginning of the case, former Prime Minister Chautemps knew everything, but he (Chautemps) tried to cover it up and used the method of shifting the line of sight to eliminate the case. Before September 1933, Chautemps had already known the details of the Stavisky case, although there were rumors outside at the time, Chautemps did not strictly order the arrest. Most of the Radical Socialist Party members helped Stavisky, and the prosecutor and the administrative organs were Stavisky's amulet. Former Minister of Labor Dalimier even helped Stavisky with an official letter (referring to the official letter of the Ministry of Labor, agreeing that the Social Insurance Bank should purchase the false bonds of Bayonne City). Chautemps served as Minister of the Interior and Prime Minister from June 1932 to January 1934. How could he know nothing about this case? Tiddio then proved that many of Chautemps' staff knew Stavisky well. The detective team had all the files on Stavisky, which were locked in a secret place by senior officials, and treated as national secrets. Tiddio then said that Chautemps used various means to make Stavisky free from legal sanctions, and Stavisky was able to escape on December 23 last year. After listening to Tiddio's statement, the investigation committee decided to hold a meeting at 9 pm to let Tiddio confront Chautemps. Tiddio's testimony made a deep impression on the investigation committee. Most members believed that Tiddio's declaration would not only have an impact on the work of the investigation committee, but also cause repercussions in the general political situation, because it would be enough to cause debates among various political parties. In the lounge of the House of Representatives, the public was quite moved by Tiddio's words. Radical Socialist and Socialist Party members disagreed with Tiddio's words, while Tiddio's friends expressed their approval. In short, Tiddio's testimony is likely to cause major political repercussions. (Havas News, 18th)

Taipei, Southern Taiwan, and the East Coast have experienced a major typhoon since yesterday morning, coupled with drizzling rain. It has temporarily calmed down by this evening. Poland and Czech Republic Suffer from Flood and Drought Disasters 60

Poland Experiencing the Worst in a Century　　Czech Government Orders Exemption of Land Rent

Poland has suffered the worst floods in over a century, with huge losses of life and property. It is said that the death toll has exceeded 100 people, and the material losses will leave tens of thousands of farmers destitute. The flooded area is expanding day by day. The water from the Vistula River has exceeded the usual water level by 16.5 feet. The army is now assisting residents of Krakow and Tarnow in the south to relocate, and is trying to rescue thousands of trapped students from a place cut off from all sides. 200 Boy Scouts have been living in trees for the past three days, sleeping on branches at night, with water flowing under the trees. (Reuters News, 18th)

Czech Republic The Czech Republic has also been suffering from prolonged drought this year, resulting in poor agricultural production. The Czech government has therefore issued an order to suspend all rent payments for tenants. This legal decree is effective until September 30. Prior to this order, the Czech government also issued a similar order on May 9 to protect farmers from landlords' extortion and relocation. Therefore, this order is actually a continuation of the previous method. (National News, 18th)

Severe Drought in the Midwestern United States 61

Kansas City The climate in the Midwestern United States is extremely hot and has not rained for a long time. A drought has formed, which may be the worst disaster in many years. In the past few days, the temperature in the shade has reached 117 degrees, coupled with 27 days without rain, the situation is becoming more serious. There is no hope that the heat will subside soon. Many industries have stopped, and people and animals are feeling distressed. The slaughterhouses here are extremely busy, because farmers are driving their livestock to the market to be slaughtered. Oklahoma City shot 600 head of livestock, because they suffered too much and died in pain. It is better to kill them to reduce their pain. Many places lack drinking water, and daily water use is limited. Schools here have all been closed. (Telecommunications News, 19th)

National Government Decree

Prohibiting Additional Taxes on Salt 62

(Nanjing) The National Government issued an order on the 19th, stating that salt tax is a national income and should be collected uniformly by the Ministry of Finance for overall planning and consolidation. Local governments must not establish additional taxes under other names. This was ordered by the Executive Yuan in December of the 19th year of the Republic of China and circulated for compliance. It is now reported by the Executive Yuan that although the previous prohibition order has been faithfully implemented by some provinces, there are also some who have disobeyed the order and continue to collect taxes as usual. This situation is enough to hinder the unification of national taxes. Senior military and political officials of each province should order their respective subordinate agencies and local groups to strictly abide by the previous order and never establish any additional taxes on salt. County magistrates should be responsible for supervising at any time and strictly preventing such practices, in order to emphasize national taxes and avoid divergences. This order. (Central News Agency, 19th)

79th Day Reuters Special Business Intelligence Telegram 84

≈Gold and Silver≈ The listed price of gold in London today is 137 shillings and 10 pence, 2 pence lower than yesterday.

The Jinan Police Cracks Down on a

Counter-Revolutionary Military Organization 101

Using Yimin Company as a Cover, Company Stock Certificates Were Used to Appoint Fake Military Commanders, and All Have Been Arrested. Jinan Correspondence: Recently, some disillusioned military personnel secretly organized a large-scale counter-revolutionary organization in Shandong Province, appointing a large number of military division and brigade commanders, recruiting and organizing troops in various counties, intending to launch a major uprising. This was truly shocking. The special investigation team of the Military Law Department of the Third Route Army Headquarters cracked the case, and today (17th), they were escorted to the Military Law Department of the Third Route Army Headquarters for interrogation. The details of the process are described below:

Organizational Content: In June of this year, the Shandong authorities received a confidential report stating that some disillusioned military personnel were secretly working in the province, mobilizing troops, and intending to launch a major uprising. Liu Yaoting, the captain of the special investigation team of the Third Route Army Headquarters, immediately dispatched detectives to investigate in detail and attempted to infiltrate the organization in order to obtain evidence. They learned that these disillusioned military personnel did not use military titles on the surface and were operating under the name of Yimin Company. Everything was replaced with stocks, with 10,000 yuan worth of stock being the equivalent of a division commander, 5,000 yuan worth of stock being the equivalent of a brigade commander, and so on. The general manager on the stock certificates was You Renxiao, and the deputy manager was Huang Ziliang, who were the actual commander and deputy commander. They also appointed Shu Zhentang, who was accustomed to mobilizing troops, as the commander of the First Army. Below him were five divisions: Ren Buyuan, the commander of the First Division; Wang Zhongting, the commander of the Second Division; Liu Junming, the commander of the Third Division; Liu Yanbin, the commander of the Fourth Division; and Bu Hanzhang, the commander of the Fifth Division. Zhang Huchen was the commander of the First Brigade of the First Division; Wang Zhizhong was the commander of the Second Brigade; and Lü Xianbin was the commander of the Third Brigade. They were recruiting troops throughout the province, plotting a major uprising.

The Entire Case is Cracked: After the investigation team learned the content of the fake organization, they secretly investigated the location of its key personnel. On the 14th of this month, Shu Zhentang, the fake army commander, was arrested at No. 104 Wangguanzhuang near Xinzhuang. The fake Yimin Company stock certificates representing the appointment of Shu Zhentang as the Jinan manager and the appointment of Shu Zhentang as the lieutenant general commander of the First Army of the Third Route Army were found. The lists of names made by the division and brigade commanders and the submissions from the various divisions and brigades reporting the recruitment of troops were also found. Hou Zhenhuan, who was also involved in the activities and impersonating a military officer, was also arrested. Yue Dai, the commander of the First Brigade, and two suspects, Si Shizhai and Wang Fengwen, were arrested in Yuanliuzhuang, along with four stock certificates. Xie Guangsong, a relative of the deputy commander, was arrested in the Big Locust Tree area of Jinan and brought to the team headquarters. With the evidence in hand, they all confessed to the crimes. After the 1,000 witnesses and evidence were escorted to the Military Law Department on the 17th, it was reported that Han Fuju will personally interrogate them. The various fake documents seized are copied below:

(1) The Fake Headquarters Order Requesting the Creation of a Roster: "Order to Know the Magistrate: According to the General Command Order No. 1, this is an order to inform the magistrate that the names, ages, and origins of the various division and brigade commanders of the First Army of this route are to be promptly reported in detail for record and reference. The various divisions are ordered to instruct their subordinates to comply with this order. This order. The right is to order Ren Buyuan, the commander of the First Division; Wang Zhongting, the commander of the Second Division; Liu Junming, the commander of the Third Division; Liu Yanbin, the commander of the Fourth Division; and Bu Hanzhang, the commander of the Fifth Division, to comply. Shu Zhentang, Army Commander, July 10, 23rd year of the Republic of China."

(2) Roster of Senior Military Officers of the Fake First Division: Ren Buyuan, the commander of the Fake First Division, submitted a list of names of his subordinate brigade commanders, saying, "For submission and hopeful examination. The names, origins, and ages of the brigade commanders of my division are listed in detail and respectfully submitted for your review and approval. Please forward this to the headquarters for record and reference. Submitted by Ren Buyuan, Commander of the First Division, to Army Commander Shu. July 11, 23rd year of the Republic of China. List as follows: Zhang Huchen, Commander of the First Brigade, from Maojia Village, south of Puzhou County, Shandong Province, 44 years old this year; Wang Zhizhong, Commander of the Second Brigade, from the north of Yuncheng County, Shandong Province, 47 years old this year; Lü Xianbin, Commander of the Third Brigade, from Majia Village, north of Pei County, Jiangsu, 46 years old this year."

(3) Wang Zhongting, commander of the Fake First Division, submitted his origin, age, and origin, saying, "Respectfully submitted to Army Commander Shu for your examination. I, Wang Zhongting, am 43 years old, from Licheng County. I came from the 3rd Battalion, 19th Biao, Zheng Bing, of the Changmin Minjun in the 34th year of Guangxu. I graduated from the Officer Company in the first year of Xuantong and was promoted to platoon leader of the 19th Biao. In the 13th year of the Republic of China, I was the commander of the Yanzhou Guard Regiment of the 16th Mixed Brigade of the Yuwan Guerrilla Force. Submitted by Wang Zhongting, July, year of the Republic of China."

(4) The Commander of the Fourth Division submitted, "For the purpose of reporting the number of soldiers recruited and the number of firearms, and earnestly requesting the issuance of appointment certificates for office use. Since Yanbin sent personnel to recruit in various counties in recent days, it has been reported that a brigade has been recruited in Lijin Luhua, Huimin, Teng County, Zou County, and Yixian, a brigade has been recruited in Shan County, Jinxiang, Yutai, and Jiaxiang, and a brigade has been recruited in Jining, Wenshang, and Yuncheng. , Liangshan and other places, a total of about 10,000 soldiers, and 50% of the firearms can be adequately provided, and the number of people has not changed, etc. According to this, I earnestly request the issuance of a division commander's appointment to facilitate office work. It is really convenient, Presented by Army Commander Shu, Liu Yanbin presented respectfully, June, year of the Republic of China."

(5) Fake military officers reported their resumes and assembly locations, "Respectfully presented to Army Commander Shu for review. Zhao Senlin is 48 years old, from Tai'an. He came from the 3rd company of the 93rd regiment of the 47th brigade in January. He was promoted to platoon leader of the 3rd battalion of the New Army, and then promoted to the 12th company commander, a major adjutant in the 13th Division of the Allied Forces. Assembly location: Dong'a, Dongping, Pingyin, Feicheng, Lijin, etc. I, Xing Youliang, am 34 years old, from Zhejiang. He came from the 13th Army commander in the 13th year of the Republic of China, and then changed to the battalion commander of the 13th Army. Assembly location: Yanggu, Shouzhang, Changqing, Qihe, Gaotang, Xiajin. I, Chen Xiyu, am 28 years old, from Mengyin County. He came from the 121st Brigade adjutant of the Northeast Army, and was a major adjutant of the Northeast Army in the 16th year. Later, he was promoted to commander of the guard regiment. Assembly location: Mengyin, Xintai, Yishui, Laiwu, July, year of the Republic of China."

(6) Stock Text of Yimin Company, that is, the Fake Headquarters: "Yimin Company Limited, now there is Mr. □, who invests and cooperates with a capital of 5,000 yuan to promote technology and expand business, and recognizes the regulations proposed by the directors as appropriate, and mutual assistance is the purpose. Our company sincerely accepts it, and now it has received an investment of 5,000 yuan without error, and issues a stock certificate as evidence. From the day of opening, it will be the time for the company to expand. This ticket should be kept as evidence, and the articles of association are attached separately. General Manager You Renxiao, Associate Manager Huang Ziliang, year month day of the Republic of China." (Note: The 5,000 yuan stock is for the brigade commander, and the 10,000 yuan stock is for the division commander.)

(7) Fake military commander Shu Zhentang's stock appointment certificate, Yimin Company's letter of engagement: "Now we hire Shu Zhentang as the manager of Yimin Company in Jinan, Please

(8) Appointment of Shu as Lieutenant General, and Letter of Appointment from the Third Route Army Headquarters: "Civil Character No. 1, I hereby appoint Shu Zhentang as the Lieutenant General of the First Army of the Shu Route. This letter, Commander-in-Chief You Renxiao, Deputy Commander Huang Ziliang, Month and Day of the year of the Republic of China." (17th)

Female Bandit Zhen Hui Surrenders and

Bitterly Narrates the Crimes of the Bandit Troops 102

The True Face of Economic Bankruptcy is Fully Revealed. The National Army's Policy Change is a Fatal Blow.

Nanchang Communication: Military Information. The surrendered female bandit, Zhen Hui, described the ills of the Communist bandits in great detail. The details are as follows:

1. Suicide Policy: The Communist bandits follow Lenin's theory and imitate Soviet Russia's strategy, but they implement it blindly and brutally without considering the facts. They also want to complete their tasks quickly using mechanized methods. On the outside, they still use the slogan of developing the national revolutionary war as a slogan, but inside the bandit areas, they are carrying out a proletarian dictatorship. Those who come from the so-called bourgeoisie and the majority of the petty bourgeoisie are not allowed to survive in the bandit areas. Even those who have a long history in a bandit party and have been responsible for important responsibilities are severely attacked. Or, under the pretext of errors in work or theory, they are killed without any politeness. According to his analysis, except for a very small number of farm laborers who are proletarians, most of the self-cultivating farmers are also regarded as petty bourgeoisie. Workers with slightly higher wages are said to be capitalist lackeys and aristocratic workers. Then, in China, which has a universal small-scale peasant economic organization and an undeveloped industry, if it is to be carried out under the policy of the Communist bandits, it can only be to kill all 400 million Chinese compatriots. This inhumane policy has already determined its natural demise in China's economic organization.

2. Contradiction of Labor Law: Generally, workers in the bandit areas must be subject to their labor laws. However, the labor laws in the bandit areas are completely a kind of legislation that treats employers harshly. For example, every boss who has 80 yuan of capital must be introduced to a worker by the Soviet to work for him. Both parties sign a contract. If it is a child laborer, the monthly wage must be 10 to 12 yuan, and they must often participate in Soviet meetings and work, and the wage is still paid. Within a month, they must not work for the boss for more than half a month. Therefore, the boss has no choice but to close the door, and the worker has no choice but to lose his job. Therefore, the herding workers in the bandit areas are all unemployed under the influence of their labor laws. On the other hand, the industry in the bandit areas cannot be developed. These are all contradictions that arise from their actions without considering the facts.

3. Economic Bankruptcy: The Communist bandits have been through the National Army's first, second, third, fourth, and fifth encirclement and suppression campaigns. Although they have not been completely eliminated,

However, the scope of the bandit areas is shrinking day by day. In addition to the blockade policy and the fierce war, the strong men in the bandit areas are all conscripted into the bandit army, and the productivity has been sharply reduced. The problem of economic materials has caused great panic. According to the pseudo-central statistics, the expenditure table of each bandit area must be at least one million or so per month. In the Xiang, E, and Gan bandit areas, the food allowance of two yuan per month per person cannot be issued. There is no way to intensify the guerrilla warfare, capture the local tyrants, and even peel off the skin of the local tyrants in the guerrilla area. They can only oppress the masses and sell public bonds. The public bonds have already been issued for four periods. The masses have already received a piece of worthless paper several times and are unwilling to be fooled again. Therefore, the economic crisis in the bandit areas is deepening day by day. 4. The Mask of Deception is Unveiled: The Communist bandits have always used the trick of deceiving the masses with the issue of political power and land, in order to seize the masses as a way to fight for their sphere of influence and die. But in fact, because their entire economic problem cannot be solved, the nameless exploitation of the masses is beyond description. What progressive tax, mutual aid association fees, and fundraising, each mass must store a basket of grain, a pound of oil, and half a catty of salt for the bandit army, and every woman must make shoes for the bandit army, beat grass horses, send fruits, donate cotton clothes, and also cultivate public fields and fields of the bandit army family for the bandit army. What sentry duty, conscription, meetings, stretcher teams, transportation teams, and so on, are all forced to come. If they resist, they will be charged with counter-revolution, and the masses will suffer from hunger and cold, cry out bitterly, and their lives are miserable beyond description. Because of this, under the influence of seven points of politics in the fifth encirclement and suppression campaign, a very large number of the masses turned back to the banner of the Blue Sky and White Sun to find a way out. 5. Factional Division: Inside the Communist bandits, due to the disunity of political propositions and the excessive intensity of class struggle, a large number of factional organizations have occurred, such as the reorganization faction, the AB group, the love research society, the Third Party, the cancellation faction, the left leaning, the right leaning, the opportunism Li San line, the Luo Ming line, and other names. These people are fighting each other, which is a symbol of his tangible collapse.

6. Ideological Shaking: Those who have a little thought are shaking politically because they see that the strategies being carried out by the Communist Party cannot adapt to the current Chinese struggle which is too intense, and ideological shaking occurs. Shaking produces factions, and factions produce struggles. The result of the struggle is mutual loss and injury, or being killed, or being arrested, or running away. People with simple thoughts are shaking purely because their lives are too hard and the discipline is too strict. They just want to drag their guns and surrender in exchange for money to go home.

7. The Fatal Wound of the Communist Bandits: The Communist Bandits have always believed that any difficulty that is tangible can be overcome with a tenacious and arduous spirit. Only intangible enemies, if not encountered, are fine, but if encountered, they become a fatal wound. What they fear most is the improvement of policies. Now, suppressing bandits with seven points of politics has already given him a fatal wound. In the current society that has not yet established the country with morality, practicing the New Life Movement, improving personal integrity, and promoting the Three People's Principles that are suitable for the national conditions, has given a great blow to the policy background of the Communist Bandits in an intangible way. He has no way to save his demise. As for the strong men in the bandit areas, who have died almost to the last one, and the lack of a source of supply of materials and military supplies, this is an inevitable phenomenon in all bandit areas. (July 17th)

Severe Drought in Jiangxi Province 103

The Fields Are Cracked and the Early Rice is Withered. The Price of Rice in Nanchang City Has Already Soared. Nanchang Communication: Since the several heavy rains before the Dragon Boat Festival in this province caused floods in the Xiu, Yuan, Rui, Fu, Rao, Xin, Ji, and Gan rivers, there has been no rain since then, for more than a month now, without a single drop. The heat continues to rise and increase, and it has reached above 100 degrees before the Little Heat. The hotter the climate, the faster the moisture evaporates. The water level of the Gan River has dropped, just like in winter. The ponds and ports are even worse. At the beginning of June in the lunar calendar, the temperature in this city is often between 104 and 106 degrees, breaking the record of decades. The drought in various places is becoming more and more serious. All the early rice can still be harvested. Farmers along the rivers, lakes, and those who have dug ponds and wells can rescue the rice with water day and night. However, the soil in the higher fields and those that mature later is cracked, the color of the rice is withered and yellow, and there is no way to save it. There is no water to draw for those who have planted the late rice, and there is no water to transplant for those who have not planted it. The bankrupt rural areas are covered with another heavy mist. Especially since the bandit disaster in Jiangxi has lasted for seven or eight years, what can be more disastrous than this severe drought in the midst of bandit and flood disasters? At about 4:00 PM on the 16th of this month, the sky was filled with clouds, followed by a strong north wind. Everyone looked forward to it, thinking that they could fill the land with sweet rain. However, after a few drops of rain fell, the clouds dispersed and the sky cleared. The rain was not smooth yesterday and today, and it did not help the agricultural affairs. In the past few days, the price of rice has risen from six yuan to seven yuan and several jiao. The well water is shallow and dry, and the river water is expensive. There is a problem with the drinking water for civilians. In addition, during the drought and heat, epidemics are rampant. The provincial health department is conducting epidemic prevention injections in five districts of the city. The public security bureau strictly prohibits coolies from sleeping in the open. The authorities have taken two pumps in the city and lent them to the water conservancy bureau to pump water in the Fu River for the drought relief issue, but there are no other practical methods. The farmers are at a loss, and they can only lift the Bodhisattva to ask for rain. (17th)

Qingjiang's Prolonged Drought Has Resulted in a Famine

There is No Hope for the Autumn Harvest in the North Countryside 104

Qingjiang is a county in Jiangxi Province that produces rice. Every year, the grain produced is more than enough for the local people to eat. In mid-June of this year, a river flood broke out, causing a vast expanse of water. After the water receded, it was followed by seasonal rain, causing the pools and lakes to be full of water. The farmers in the east, west, and south of the county were all overjoyed, celebrating the signs of a good harvest year, meaning that even if it did not rain for half a month from now, they would not be without water to draw. However, the land in the north countryside is low-lying, and it has the name of a water village. When the water rises, the early rice is submerged. The private dikes built around the countryside are counted in numbers, and those that have been washed down by the water are still half-flooded. Not only is there no hope for the autumn harvest, but also the current life is very difficult. As for the east, west, and south, because there has been no rain for a long time recently, the stored water has been used up and there is no water to irrigate. They are sitting and waiting to die. If there is still some remaining water available for irrigation, they work day and night, and their hands and feet are calloused, so that the rice can be expected to survive. But the farmers are exhausted and have already lost more than they gained. In addition, most of the rice crops show signs of withering. The scorching heat has not subsided, and the signs of famine have already appeared. The people in the cities and villages are now looking forward to the rain, and they are using various superstitious methods to ask for rain. Unfortunately, the sweet rain is still not falling. The rice merchants in Zhangshu have already raised the price of rice by two or three yuan. If it does not rain again, the people's food will be very worrying. (Shenbao Correspondence, Huang Sijian, Student of Yuan School)

(Northwest Inspection Record) Our newspaper's special correspondent, Geng Ya

Arriving in Lanzhou 105

June 3rd: Departed from Shiguaizi and Wulishahui well. Due to rushing the previous day, the horse was exhausted and unable to proceed, so another one was hired and sent to Lanzhou for a price of four yuan. The land here needs to be left fallow to replenish its fertility, and some even leave it for two or three years, otherwise it is futile. At Ganlu Pond, 20 li away, I studied with an old farmer about the method of planting with sand, which can be used as fertilizer. The reasons are roughly: (1) The stone has a moistening air, which can nourish crops; (2) After rain, it can retain moisture and does not dry for a long time; (3) During storms, it can suppress the roots of crops; (4) The soil is firm and dry, and lacks fertilizer, so it is difficult to expect a harvest without laying sand and stones. However, the sand-laying project is vast, and each mu of land requires a layer of three or four cun thick, costing more than sixty gold coins. Moreover, the effect of new laying is slight, and the power declines over time. The prosperous period is only twenty or thirty years, at most fifty or sixty years, and then it must be discarded and replaced. Therefore, there is a saying: "The old man suffers to death, the son eats to death, and the grandson starves to death." In other provinces, when cultivating, if there are sand and stones, they must be removed, but here it is the opposite. Although it is said to be suitable for the land, it is not a good method after all. Moreover, it is said that "how thick the sand is, how deep the cultivation is." If it is not sandy land, it is only shallow cultivation of two or three cun, which is very different from the method of deep cultivation. Most of the fields in Gansu Province are widely planted and sparsely harvested, and not knowing deep cultivation is a major reason. It is not only the lack of water.

The population in the village was originally lush and dense. In the eighteenth year of the drought, nearly half of the people starved to death. Now the fields are barren, year after year. On the one hand, it is due to the sparse population, and on the other hand, it is due to the lack of capital for cultivation. Before the eighteenth year, ordinary interest rates, although as high as 50% to 100%, were painfully exploited, but there was still a place to borrow. But since the eighteenth year, the entire people have been impoverished. If there are any savings, in order to avoid the coveting of the poor and the excessive burden of errands, they all pretend to be poor to block the door for borrowing. Farmers, in order to purchase seeds and other emergency needs, even if they mortgage their property at several times the interest rate, no one dares to respond. As a result, they miss the farming season and force people to death everywhere. To make it recover, a credit cooperative is needed.

At Liudunzi, 20 li away, there are sixty or seventy households. The well is twelve zhang deep, and someone specializes in the job of drawing water. The method is to place a simple pulley on the well, tie a bucket with a rope, and lower it into the well. At the other end, livestock are used to pull the rope, going as far as twelve zhang. The bucket rises, pours water, and returns to its original place. One person controls the bucket, and one person drives the animals back and forth. It is very time-consuming and labor-intensive. Villagers pay one sheng of wheat per person per year for drinking water, and one he (approximately two jiao and five fen) per animal per month. Travelers who water their horses pay five copper coins per head each time. If there is a drought and the spring dries up, it is even more expensive than nectar. Therefore, to revitalize agriculture, water conservancy is the primary issue. Whether storing mountain floods or using machines to draw well water, it is not easy to do without huge capital.

The area of land is mostly measured in "chang," with each "chang" approximately equal to two and a half mu, worth forty or fifty yuan. If wheat is planted, the annual harvest is two or three dou, worth about fourteen or fifteen yuan. If poppies are planted, five or sixty liang of opium gum can be harvested, worth about thirty yuan. However, compared to planting wheat, it requires five yuan more fertilizer and eleven or twelve yuan more labor. If the harvest is small or the price falls, it is not as profitable as planting wheat. The above-mentioned yield refers to ordinary new sandy land. If it is old sandy land, I am afraid there will be no such harvest. The field tax is five he of grain per chang, worth about thirty cents in silver, plus one yuan for Qingxiang fees, and about three yuan per year for errands and miscellaneous expenses. The income and expenditure are mostly insufficient. Therefore, there is a saying in the local area: "Farmers do not calculate accounts, but calculate how full their bellies are."

At Sandunzi, 30 li away, we stayed overnight at sunset. That day, we traveled a total of 75 li. The residents, sixty or seventy households, had returned from farming and herding, and it was already dark. Most of them held bowls and drank noodle soup under the starlight in front of the eaves. There is a street running east and west, about a li long, with houses lined up, but only three families can be seen with lights on. I stayed in a horse inn, where the manure and grass in the earthen trough were close to the room. There were no windows to sleep, and the stench was overwhelming. The kang was piled with dust, and the wall lamp was dim. Someone jokingly wrote a poem about this scene: "Earthen kang and stone pillow, lamp oil flows down the wall (a broken bowl bottom is used as a lamp, placed high in the wall hole, the oil overflows and flows down, the wall slides with black ditches, and the pit collects it, which can be used again), one night of feeling lice, all night of listening to horse urine." It can be called a living painting.

On the 4th, because I wanted to rush to Lanzhou, I left Sandunzi at 3:00 AM. Initially, I entered the mountains and did not see open space for a long time. The road is divided into a highway and a post road. The highway is high, wide, and flat, while the post road is low, concave, and rugged. Many vehicles abandoned the post road and took the highway without permission. The road bureau could not prohibit it, so they dug deep drainage ditches in the middle of the highway. Cars could still pass, but horse-drawn carriages were stuck in a dilemma, inevitably trapping the wheels or stumbling the horses. We were caught in their trap and could not extricate ourselves. I deeply regret that the pit was not dug at the beginning of the road, but in the middle, and that the post road was not repaired, so that the sedan carriers avoided difficulties and took the easy way, often mistakenly falling into deep pits. This is not the intention of a benevolent person. The ground beside the road is full of mouse holes. Measuring the distance, there is one hole every two square feet. The entrances of the holes are all newly placed wheat seedlings or artemisia grass, which are the leftovers from the mice's food. If most of the crops are poppies, and there are one or two mu of wheat ears that are just ripening, the mice will gather in hundreds and thousands, and they will be able to destroy them completely in one day and night. This is not only for their immediate consumption, but also mostly dragged into the holes and stored as winter food. Therefore, the harm of mice is more severe than locusts. There are crows with bright red beaks and distances, which are said to be able to prey on small mice, but the effect is minimal.

At Shuibu River, 70 li away, there are fifty or sixty residents. The stream is clear and the willows line the banks, a pleasant scenery rarely seen since entering Gansu. I had "liangfen" for lunch, each small bowl costing one jiao. In Beijing, it would only be worth two or three fen. I asked why the price of snacks was so high, and how could the people afford to eat? The answer was: "Villagers mostly eat wheat bran, wild vegetables, or yam eggs. The beans, wheat flour, soy sauce, vinegar, etc. used to make this liangfen and liangmian are all purchased from Gaolan. The villagers really have no ability to buy food." The gentlemen traveling with me ate fried rice, and the number of people watching with drooling mouths increased. The eaters were embarrassed and wanted to stop. An old man smiled sadly and said, "Our land has not seen rice since the three years of drought, which is almost ten years. How can we want to eat it?" The fried rice was originally brought from Zhongwei, to be prepared for the lack of food at the Sisha station. Now that the sand station has passed, and Lanzhou is in sight, why carry it? So it was distributed to the onlookers, who were all happy and grateful. Someone said, "This is not enough to be miserable. In various counties in Longxi, people pile hot sand in pits in winter, and people lie in it to keep warm. Girls over ten years old still have bare legs and no pants to wear. In the past, people sold their sons and daughters, and someone would buy them, but now no. Because those who bought other people's sons and daughters in the past now also want to sell their wives and daughters, but they are suffering from having no way to do so. Therefore, relief is more urgent than development, which is true for the entire Northwest, and especially true for Gansu. Who says it is not appropriate?"

Horse-drawn carriages used in the Northwest provinces

At Sandao Xian, 15 li away, the slope goes up and down three times, as steep as a ladder to the sky. The road around the Erdao Xian peak is especially dangerous, as it is occupied by bandits. At the foot of the slope is a mountain village, where poppies are budding and about to bloom, and wheat seedlings have sprouted ears. The tombs are planted with many trees, with tall trunks reaching the sky, providing cool shade. However, the village and mountain areas are bare without a single green tree. I flicked my whip, wanting to find a branch but could not. At Zhongbaozi, 15 li away, the Gaolan Mountain stretches across the clouds, towering in sight. About fourteen of the twenty households in the village live in caves. Leaving Zao Yuan, I went down along a well, with dangerous cliffs on both sides. About fourteen households live in caves. Leaving Jiyuan, I went along roads made into blocks, plastered on the walls, and exposed to the sun to be used as fuel. At Lanzhou, 15 li away, it was already night. The electric lights shone like a painting. The sound of the Yellow River was very loud, making people feel silent. The city gate was closed, and I stayed overnight at Jincheng Pass. That day, I traveled a total of 140 li. The next morning, I entered the city and settled in the Zhonghua Hotel. In total, the journey from Ning to Lan was more than 1,200 li, with fourteen horse stations. When the car is running, it will arrive in four days. The Ninglan air service is even more convenient.

County government reports on disaster relief planning

Songjiang 106

Since the beginning of summer, the heat has been increasing, and there has been no rain for a long time, causing the crops to wither. The farmers in each township are worried about the drought and are planning to remedy it. Fortunately, since the 10th, there has been light rain every day, which has provided some moisture. County Magistrate Jin recently telegraphed to the heads of the three departments of the Provincial Government Chairman, People's Finance, and Construction, reporting that "Since the beginning of summer in Songyi, there has been very little rainfall. According to statistics, in more than seventy days, only 131.7 millimeters of rainfall have been received. In the past month, the temperature has been unusually high, and the scorching sun has evaporated the water, causing the agricultural rivers to dry up and the land to crack. At this time, the seedlings are just being planted, and farming is in full swing. The villagers work hard day and night, but they suffer from the difficulty of drawing water and the limited effectiveness. The cattle are overworked and die frequently. On the 12th of this month, there was a brief shower in Xinzhuang, a village in the east, but it cleared up immediately. If it does not rain again, it will lead to a drought. As the county magistrate, it is my duty to plan day and night and dare not be negligent. In addition to the prevention of locusts and famine, I have followed the repeated orders and instructed the competent authorities to actively plan for contingencies. It has been found that a small number of fields in Pubei are in urgent need of relief due to the difficulty of drawing water. Although the current situation in other places can be barely maintained, it cannot last for long. Punan, on the other hand, has a higher terrain, and the signs of disaster have already appeared, especially in the areas of Shanyang Caojing and the southern part of Tinglin. Previously, I convened Chen Xingyuan, the manager of the Agricultural Extension Institute, Ding Zhenya, the cooperation instructor, and invited Li Jiannong, the president of the Farmers Bank, to study the methods of drought prevention and disaster relief in detail. The general decisions were: (1) The Agricultural Extension Institute will send staff to investigate the fields in Shanyang Caojing and the southern part of Tinglin that have not been planted and have died of drought, and prepare to replant buckwheat and green beans. The funds for purchasing seeds will be allocated from the business expenses of the Extension Institute. (2) The county government will first purchase four water pumping machines, which will cost approximately four thousand yuan, and borrow them from the farmers at interest. These water pumping machines will be rented and used by the people in the disaster-stricken areas. The detailed methods have been decided at the 22nd Political Affairs Meeting. The matter of borrowing funds from the Farmers Bank has also been telegraphed for approval. This is the general situation of the severe drought in Songyi since the beginning of summer, and the planned prevention and rescue measures. On the 18th of this month, 15.5 millimeters of rain fell in the urban area. According to telephone inquiries, most of the townships in Pubei have also received timely rain of varying amounts. If it continues to rain extensively, most of the farmland is expected to recover. The purchase of pumping machines can be temporarily postponed. However, the fields in the south that have died of drought must be replanted with buckwheat and green beans as soon as possible to compensate for the losses. I have already ordered the Extension Institute to actively handle it. All the dried-up agricultural rivers have also been ordered to be dredged as soon as possible to facilitate irrigation. This is the general situation of the long-term drought in Songyi and the urgent handling of the situation. In addition to continuing to plan and handle things according to circumstances, I am aware of the situation and respectfully report the severe drought in Songyi since the beginning of summer, the planned prevention and rescue measures, and the handling of the aftermath of the long-term drought and rain. Jin Tigan, County Magistrate of Songjiang, bows." Watergate sets up water station for drought relief

Suzhou 107

Suzhou has not received adequate rainfall for two months, causing great impact on drinking water and farmland. Although there has been occasional light rain recently, it has not been of practical help. The county government, in view of this, specially followed the provincial government's meeting to decide on drought relief measures. First, a water station was set up in Xukou, building dikes to divert water. Yesterday (19th), a notice was specially issued to ships traveling to and from the area, ordering them to stop navigation to implement the construction project. At the same time, Wang Kanggu, an engineer from the Construction Department, was allowed to say that the flood dam between Taihu Lake and Yunhu Lake in Wangting District had an urgent need to be opened. Therefore, the district chief of the fourth district of Wangting, Lu, has been ordered to raise 150 workers on a deadline to wait for dispatch.

Demolishing floodgates to relieve drought

Wuxi 108

Wang Yuangu, an engineer from the Jiangsu Construction Department, was ordered to come to Wuxi to preside over the extraction of river and lake water sources to relieve the drought. Accompanied by Huang Dechun, the technical section chief of the county construction bureau, he inspected the water flow at Liangxikou, Taibaodun, and Li Bridge. Yesterday morning (18th) at about 7:00 AM, Engineer Wang, Section Chief Huang, and Xia Shouzheng, an engineer transferred from the Construction Department to Wuxi for assistance, took a car to Wangting to inspect the water level of Wangting Bridge. The river there is currently flowing towards Suzhou to the east. They then went to Xiangshui Bridge and Tonghu Bridge, Changzhao Canal, floodgates, and other places for inspection. Then they went to Shadun Port and the Shaduntou area for inspection and measurement. It was estimated that the current water volume in the port is about two meters deep or more, and the width of the inlet is 25 meters, with a depth of about 1.5 meters. The natural water flow is still sufficient, so Engineer Wang believes that there is no need to set up a station. However, the exit of the port is directly connected to the Grand Canal. Because the water flow was rapid and rushed into the Grand Canal, hindering the safety of navigation, a floodgate was specially built. The only way for the port's water to exit is at Xiangshui Bridge. The bridge has three bridge holes, with a total width of less than five meters. Therefore, the water flow is difficult, and the water level inside and outside differs by as much as one foot. The solution is to open the floodgate so that the water volume can flow smoothly and unhindered. The northwest can flow to the northeastern townships of Xijing, and the southwest can flow to Suzhou. Demolition began yesterday (19th). The required project funds will be temporarily advanced by the county. Engineer Wang personally supervised and guided the work. The dredging of the Lujiangkou River channel has been completed. The dam was removed and water was released. Regarding the problem of relieving drinking water in the urban area, the First District Office has hired a machine to pump water into the city, which costs three yuan and five jiao per hour. It is now planned to use 400 yuan of levee repair funds. The insufficient amount will be raised by the town chiefs through donations.

Climate Turns Cooler After Showers 109

Since the Minor Heat, there have been occasional hurricanes from the northwest, and the climate has turned slightly cooler, with the thermometer dropping to ninety-three or ninety-four degrees. However, the sunshine is very strong at noon. At about 2:00 PM on the 18th, the wind and clouds in the sky were urgent, and soon the darkness was dark. There was heavy rain in the middle of the sunlight, which lasted about four or five minutes. At about 5:00 PM, there was another heavy rain, which lasted for ten minutes before stopping. The southeastern part of the rural area received more rain. Kaiyuan Township, Meiyuan, Xiaojishan, and the area along Taihu Lake received two or three cun of rain. The other places, such as Nanqiao, Yuqi, Dongting, Nanfangquan, and Jiangxi Bridge, each received between one cun and two or three fen of rain. In addition, the county public security bureau, in order to remove the accumulated manure in the city, specially convened a temporary symposium yesterday to decide to recruit fifty manure collectors, entrust the fertilizer cooperative to transport them, and excavate a manure pool outside the East Gate.

Jiangsu and Zhejiang Silk Industry Discuss Standard Silk Prices 110

The silk factories in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces have suffered setbacks due to the recent sharp decline in the silk market. When the spring silkworms entered the market this year, the domestic silk price was still worth more than 500 yuan per dan, but recently it has fallen to 87 yuan. One of the reasons is the sluggishness of the European and American silk markets. However, the industry groups are not strong and there is no officially set price or powerful restraint, which has led to panic and a willingness to sell at a discount. This is the main reason. Therefore, it has been decided to hold a joint meeting at the General Office of the Silk Industry on North Shanxi Road in Shanghai at 3:00 PM on the 22nd of this month to decide on the standard silk price in order to maintain the precarious silk market. Yesterday, a special letter was sent to the local silk factory association, asking them to send six representatives to attend the meeting and discuss.

Shareholders of Shenxin No. 3 Factory Oppose Departmental Reorganization 111

The Shenxin No. 3 Textile Factory yesterday presented a telegram to Wang, the President of the Nanjing Executive Yuan, Minister Kong of the Ministry of Finance, Minister Chen of the Ministry of Industry, and the Cotton Industry Control Committee of the National Economic Council in Shanghai, which stated: "Reports say that Shenxin in Shanghai will be reorganized by the Ministry, and the candidates for the committee have reportedly been internally determined. It has been found that Shenxin's factories, whether in Shanghai or Wuxi, are all operated by businessmen surnamed Sun. The No. 1, 3, and 4 factories are especially independent as unlimited liability companies limited by shares. They have all been registered with the Ministry and have been issued licenses as proof. In terms of the shareholders' responsibilities, they should be limited to each factory. As far as Wuxi is concerned, the business has been profitable and has not been in deficit, so there is no need for reorganization. If the reorganization of the Shanghai factories is extended to Wuxi, it is actually to destroy in the name of maintenance. This sets a bad example for the company. Who would dare to invest? The shareholders will never approve it. In addition to applying to Shenxin No. 3 Factory in the capacity of shareholders, we hereby declare to Shanghai that we request your review. We are urgent and cannot choose our words. We beg you to pay attention and do not disappoint our expectations. We are sending this urgently and respectfully ask for your approval. The shareholders of Shenxin No. 3 Textile Factory in Wuxi: Hua Ganchen, You Lianzeng, Hua Yizhi, Gao Zijing, Zou Cudan, Yang Shaotang, Tang Xiongyuan, Pu Wenting, Rong Tiaofu, Fan Qinlan, Xiang Yangsi, Li Guowei, Xue Mingjian, Dou Muyi, Cha Zhongkang, Jiang Xinyi, Rong Zhuoren, Rong Zhuoqiu, Rong Zhuoya, Xue Daoqing, Li Lansheng, Rong Yuqing, Rong Esheng, Rong Yuequan, Feng Qihuai, Wu Kunsheng, Mao Jianqing, et al." Three people killed by lightning in thunder and rain

Changzhou 112

Wuyi's weather is extremely dry, and farmers are eagerly awaiting rain. The day before yesterday (17th) afternoon, Heaven finally showered sweet rain. When the rain poured down, Zhang Linfa, a villager near Minghuang Town in the 8th District, and his wife, Mrs. Zhang, were working in the field. Seeing the heavy rain, they were about to return home when they were suddenly struck by lightning. The husband and wife died in the field at the same time. When their family members sent an umbrella, they found that the two were lying stiff on the ground, already dead. Also, Xu, a villager in Dongsha Village, north of Zhaizhai Bridge, was over fifty years old. He was also working in the field at the time, and suddenly encountered thunder and rain. Xu was sucked from the air to the opposite bank and killed by lightning. His whole body turned charred black. Zhenjiang Automotive and Railway Transport

Zhenjiang 113

The Beijing-Shanghai Railway and the Zhenjiang-Danyang-Jintan long-distance bus running between Zhenjiang and Jintan have been handling passenger and baggage parcel transport since March 1st of this year. The company changed its baggage free weight and overweight charge method from April 15th, and added round-trip tickets between the road bureau's joint stations. From May 25th, the bus fare was revised, and from June 25th, the parcel fare was set. The traffic department then signed three supplementary items to the joint transport contract with the company for supplementation.

However, a bamboo basket and a sickle were left on the shore. When asked by the villagers, no one knew his name. The local officials have been ordered to prepare coffins and bury them.

Gang robbed villagers and injured the owner with a knife 117

Yu Weiqing, a resident of Daliuqiao in the western countryside of Yi Lu in Jiangdu, did not return on the sixteenth night. A dozen or so bandits, holding knives, sticks, and pistols, rushed into the gate, dragged Yu's wife from the bed, extorted money, and slashed her several times. They also melted candle oil and poured it on the wounds to inflict abuse. They then searched the house and looted everything, fired a few shots, and left with a whistle. After the incident, the loss was inspected to be about 300 yuan. Southeast Township receives light rain

Six Districts Villagers Go to the County to Announce Famine

Jiaxing 123

The Wengang in each township in Jiaxing has no water, and farmers cannot irrigate. Although the Drought Prevention Committee has prepared funds to purchase machines and distribute them to farmers for pumping water, the area is vast and difficult to spread widely. Also, because port has no water, the fields with wrapping are still difficult to protect. More than 3,000 farmers in the 6th District went to the 6th District Office in the early morning of the 19th to announce the famine, all holding withered rice. District Chief Lin Nianren avoided coming out. Later, 500-600 farmers, together with Assistant Lin from the District Office, walked from Yuxian Town to Jiaxing (a journey of more than 20 miles). At 9:00 a.m., they went to the county to announce the famine. They piled withered rice on the hall and requested that the collection of grain from the scattered warehouses be stopped for disaster relief. Section Chief Li of the County Government and instructor Mei Zizhi came out as representatives to persuade the farmers to return. County Magistrate Jiang went to the countryside two days later to inspect the disaster situation. After the inspection, there will be practical methods. Until noon, everyone dispersed. When the villagers crowded into the county government, the county surveillance team and the infrastructure tunnels persuaded them separately, and the order was good.

Jiashan County Security Corps

Letter from the First District Corps Headquarters 124

To the Editor:

Upon reading the "Truth of the Risheng Lou Bloodshed Case" news in your newspaper's Jiashan news on July 16th, which stated that "Li Shi-can and Xu Mingde were transferred to the Home Guard" and "Xu Mingde and Li Shi-can knew they had caused trouble, hired a boat to escape, and took two Home Guard rifles with them," and again, the July 17th news "Major Criminals in the East Gate Bloodshed Case Arrested" which stated "after the two criminals Li Shi-can and Xu Mingde caused trouble, they took away two rifles and one short firearm," and "the two criminals were indeed found carrying firearms in the Donghu area of Pinghu," all of which are inconsistent with the facts. It has been verified that there was previously an organization of the Chengxiang Voluntary Home Guard in our district, which was then ordered to be reorganized into a Home Guard standby team. However, the standing teams of each Jia in our district were ordered to be disbanded as early as the end of February of this year. All firearms were the responsibility of each Jia to keep safe, and there were no shortages. The sections mentioned in your newspaper are entirely fictitious, likely based on mistaken rumors. Deeply concerned about causing confusion and affecting the reputation of our district corps, we are sending this special letter to correct the record. We hope you will publish it to rectify the rumors. Sincerely,

To the Editorial Department of Shanghai Shen Bao Newspaper,

First District Corps Headquarters of Jiashan County Home Guard,

July 18th.

Local News

Yu Youren to Depart for Shaanxi 125

Lu Zhong'an, a National Physician, coordinates herbal pills with the Huadong Society, reports that Yu Youren, President of the Control Yuan, made the following remarks to reporters from the Huadong Society who visited him yesterday: The three proposals to amend the Control Yuan's impeachment procedures, submitted by the five standing members of the Central Political Committee, have been resolved. This move suggests dissatisfaction with the Control Yuan. Furthermore, due to my own physical weakness and illness that has not yet recovered, I have decided to return to my ancestral home in Shaanxi within this week to recuperate. I will make a short stop when passing through Nanjing. The corner of his mouth is still slightly crooked, and Lu Zhong'an, the national physician treating him, has coordinated herbal pills for him to take after leaving Shanghai.

Tang Youren Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday 126

According to reports on the status of North China, Huang Fu remains passive, and Yin Tong is coming to Shanghai soon, according to the Far East News Agency, Tang Youren, Permanent Vice Minister of Foreign Affairs, arrived in Shanghai at 7:30 AM yesterday morning on the night express from Nanjing. After disembarking, he went directly to his residence on Gansidong Road. Around 9:00 AM, he met with Okano, a staff officer from the Japanese warship Tsushima. At 3:30 PM, Zhou Zuomin, General Manager of Jin Cheng Bank, visited him and left after about an hour of discussion. Subsequently, Tang Youren met with a reporter from the Far East News Agency and made the following remarks:

North China is Pathologically Quiet 127

Tang Youren began by saying that although the situation in North China appears to be quiet, this quiet is not normal but pathological. Within this pathological quiet, there are still hidden worries, so we cannot be overly optimistic and should strive to restore normalcy.

Huang Fu Remains Pessimistic 128

He continued, saying that Chairman Huang (Fu)'s attitude remains passive. He feels that negotiations with the Japanese are difficult. The Kwantung Army's attitude is ambiguous and lacks sincerity, constantly engaging us in minor matters while consistently prevaricating on more important issues, such as unresolved wartime negotiations. Therefore, he is currently unwilling to return north. However, the central government will not allow him to remain passive. They are now trying to resolve his difficulties so that he will not have to make excuses and can return north as soon as possible.

New Plan Rumors are Inaccurate 129

I met with Chairman Huang and Director Yin (Tong) at Mogan Mountain, only to listen to Huang's explanation of his difficulties, which I will relay to President Wang so that he can find ways to resolve them. Rumors that we had discussed a new plan for negotiations with Japan in North China and that this new plan had been approved by the central government are merely speculation.

Yin Tong Will Arrive in Shanghai Within Days 130

Tang Youren then answered a reporter's question, stating that after returning to Nanjing from Mogan Mountain, he relayed the situation to President Wang and discussed ways to resolve Huang's difficulties. He came to Shanghai because it is cooler than Nanjing and plans to stay for a few days. Within these few days, Yin will come to Shanghai from Hangzhou to meet with him. However, it is not yet determined whether Yin will return to Hangzhou or go directly north. Tang paused here, and the reporter asked if Yin's visit was to hear Tang's response regarding resolving Huang's difficulties and then relay it to Huang. Tang nodded in agreement but firmly refused to reveal the content of the response.

Abolishing the Tanggu Truce 131

Tang Youren later discussed the abolition of the Tanggu Truce, stating that the Truce was intended to be temporary and, in fact, no longer has any value. It is not impossible to abolish, but the Japanese side does not agree to the abolition unless we pay a considerable price; it cannot be abolished unconditionally. Whether our side will propose negotiations is still under consideration.

Postal Issues Remain Unresolved 132

Continuing, he stated that the rumors of a resolution to the postal issue are inaccurate. Currently, letters sent from outside the passes to inside the passes with "Manchukuo" stamps are still considered underpaid. However, many now attach Chinese stamps, purchased in bulk from inside the passes for this purpose. As for letters sent from inside the passes to outside the passes, they are stamped with Chinese stamps. However, it is unknown whether they (referring to "Manchukuo") also consider them underpaid upon arrival.

Tang to Visit Jiang in Jiangxi 133

Tang finally stated that he will soon be traveling to Lushan to escape the summer heat. During this trip, he will take the opportunity to meet with Chairman Jiang to report on everything and discuss matters.

Relief for the Shenxin Cotton Mill

Formulating a Reorganization Plan 136

=Funds to be Borrowed by the Reorganization Committee or Raised Through Public Bonds, Still Under Discussion=

According to Xin Xin News Agency, Shenxin Cotton Mill has suffered significant losses over the years due to the impact of the economic downturn. After Rong Zongjing, the general manager of the mill, announced his retirement, the Ministry of Finance, the Ministry of Industry, the National Economic Commission, the Cotton Control Commission, and other agencies took charge of the reorganization. According to reports from investigators sent to Shanghai by the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Industry, the mill's debt is more than 13 million yuan to the Bank of China and more than 8 million yuan to the Shanghai Bank. In addition to the debt, at least 2 million yuan is needed for reorganization to maintain operations. It is learned that the Ministry of Industry has submitted the investigation report to the Executive Yuan and recommended a detailed reorganization plan, roughly as follows: (1) All factories should be maintained and not shut down; (2) The distribution and planning of relief funds should be submitted to the government by the Reorganization Committee for separate solutions. Therefore, the focus of the reorganization has become an economic issue. However, the Ministry of Industry has no funds to allocate, so the Cotton Control Commission, the Ministry of Finance, and the Economic Commission must find ways to allocate funds. As for the rumor of issuing relief bonds, this was previously suggested by someone. The method of raising funds is still to be decided by the Ministry of Finance, the Economic Commission, and other agencies.

Hurricane to Strike Zhejiang Waters

Observatory Issues Warning 137

The Nanhua Wheel Stops Temporarily Mid-Journey The Observatory reports that a hurricane in the Taiwan waters is blowing northwest, and the atmospheric pressure in the Yangtze River basin is very low. The hurricane has reached the north of Taiwan and continues to move northwest. At 6:00 AM yesterday, it had reached 30 nautical miles from the intersection of 25 degrees north latitude and 122 degrees east longitude. Commercial vessels sailing to Nanhua and various coastal ports in Zhejiang are at risk of being affected. The Observatory issued a special warning. The unlisted liner Haiyan and the Nanyang ship Gongping have both received this warning and have sailed to Lot Sin Bay to anchor and avoid the hurricane and avoid unexpected dangers. At the same time, various sea vessels reported to Shanghai to temporarily suspend navigation in transit to avoid the wind. Other Nanhua liners and Zhejiang coastal merchant ships are also uniformly prevented from suspending sailing.

Officials and Civilians Actively Fight Drought 138

The City's Fire Department Mobilized to the Fullest, Drought Prevention Committee Purchases Five Machines According to the Central News Agency, the municipal government recently recognized that the weather is extremely dry, the farmland in various rural areas of the city is withered, and a disaster is imminent. It is urgent to find ways to provide relief to maintain people's livelihoods. After discussions at the municipal conference, in addition to allocating funds to purchase a large number of water pumps to be distributed to various rural areas, it was also decided to send representatives from the Public Security, Social Affairs, Finance, and Land Bureaus, as well as representatives from various rural areas, to form a Drought Prevention Committee. As it was not possible to purchase water pumps immediately, it was decided that the fire brigades of the city would send pump vehicles with strong mechanical power to pump water in various rural areas to relieve the immediate crisis. Public Security Bureau Director Wen ordered Dong Zhihe of the Fire Prevention Section of the Second Division to assign the Shanghai South District Fire Brigade Joint Association, the Zhabei Fire Brigades, the Jiangwan, Zhenru, and Gaoqiao Fire Brigades to send twelve pump trucks to be responsible for the operation. The urgent relief areas include ten districts: Shanghai South Longhua, Caohejing, Pusong, Pengpu, Yinxiang, Jiangwan, Zhenru, Gaoqiao, and Zhabei. The Pengpu and Zhabei districts have already started the relief work. After receiving the order, the fire brigades of the city were all extremely excited and willing to participate in the relief. The working conditions of the fire brigades are recorded below:

Zhabei District This district has more than 20,000 acres of farmland. A rural representative from the district, Zhao Zuolin, personally led three large pump trucks from the Zhabei First, Second, and Fourth Fire Brigades to station in the Liuying Shuodian Road area of Zhabei. Under the command of Zhabei Fire Brigade Captain Wang Baoyu, Second Fire Brigade Captain Cao Xufan, and Fourth Fire Brigade Captain Chen Yousheng, thirty firefighters pumped water in the Henghama River and used two thousand feet of leather straps to transport it to the Hujiazhai tributary. This tributary can connect to more than one hundred branches, so the farmland in Zhabei District relies entirely on this tributary for water. Since the beginning of summer, the tributary has dried up and is difficult to use. The fire brigade worked hard to pump water from 3:00 PM until 3:00 AM yesterday, totaling more than 250,000 gallons. The tributary is now more than four feet deep and has been distributed to various branches. The villagers are all overjoyed and grateful to the fire brigade.

Pengpu District The captain of the Third Fire Brigade of Zhabei led ten firefighters and drove a large pump truck to pump water from the Pengpu Town River and distribute it to various tributaries. From 3:00 PM the day before yesterday to 3:00 PM yesterday, a total of 350,000 gallons of water was pumped. The tributaries, which were originally dry, are now more than five feet deep. The villagers have obtained water and have started farming. Public Security Bureau Director Wen Hongen was very impressed with the efforts of the fire brigade officials, who worked hard in the scorching sun, and specially went to visit and comfort them yesterday afternoon, accompanied by Dong Zhihe of the Fire Prevention Section of the bureau. It is also learned that the American Paramount Pictures Company and the Mainland Zilin News Paper Office have both sent personnel to take photos to send to various countries as news material.

Drought Relief Association According to New Voice News Agency, the third meeting was held at Yiyuan at 4:00 PM yesterday to discuss detailed implementation measures. As a result, (1) it was decided to purchase three more water pumps, (2) borrowing machines from the Junpu Bureau has been negotiated and is awaiting municipal government approval, (3) machine oil, miscellaneous expenses, and dam construction fees will all be directly issued by the municipal government. It is heard that the association has purchased three water pumps from the Xintong Company, one with 14 horsepower, to be distributed to the Gaohang District for application, and the remaining two with 11 horsepower to be distributed to the Lixing and Tangqiao districts. Two machines were also purchased from the Shanghai Machinery Factory, each with 6 horsepower, to be distributed to the Yinxiang and Pusong districts. Each district will also have a representative from the Social Affairs Bureau, together with the Farmers' Association of each district, to supervise the progress daily. The goods will be delivered and transported to various districts for application today.

Zhabei Fire Brigade Joint Association According to the East China News Agency, at 8:00 PM yesterday, an emergency meeting was convened at the Baoshan Road Clubhouse to continue discussing irrigation methods. Wang Xiaolai, Wang Binyan, Feng Bingjun, Wang Heyu, Zhao Zhongbiao, Chen Yueyun, Feng Wenlie, Chen Wencu, and Chen Weihan, more than twenty of them, representatives of the Standing Committee of each fire brigade, elected Wang Binyan as chairman, reported on the purpose of the meeting and the recent work progress. The following cases were then discussed (1) Submitting to the municipal government the recent relief irrigation work; (2) Requesting the municipal Drought Prevention Committee to quickly allocate water-lifting machines to save seedlings; (3) Continuing to work hard to start relief irrigation; (4) Requesting the Standing Committee to find ways to subsidize 300 yuan of daily gasoline and oil and other incidental expenses, and the meeting adjourned at 10:00 PM.

Beijing-Shanghai Highway Long-Distance Telephone

Expected to be Fully Completed by the End of August 149

Trial calls already completed with excellent results, according to the Xin Sheng News Agency. The long-distance telephone service along the Beijing-Shanghai Highway, undertaken by the Ministry of Communications, has been under preparation for some time. Part of the project has already been completed and is scheduled to be officially open for calls. Details are as follows:

Section-by-Section Wiring 150

The Ministry of Communications, in anticipation of the opening of the Beijing-Shanghai Highway and to facilitate transportation along the route, is sponsoring the Beijing-Shanghai Highway long-distance telephone service. The route runs from Nanjing, through Jurong, Liyang, Yixing, Wuxi, Changshu, Taicang, Jiading, and Nanxiang, to Shanghai. Since the beginning of preparations, new lines have been added and old lines repaired where existing long-distance telephone poles and lines were present. Otherwise, wooden poles have been erected and new lines strung in sections.

Clear Trial Calls 151

A total of four pairs of open wire and two pairs of phantom circuit lines have been installed along the entire route. The installation has been ongoing for some time. As of yesterday morning, two pairs of open wire and one pair of phantom circuit lines have been completed. The remaining two open wire and one phantom circuit lines are still being laid. It is expected that the entire project will be completed by the end of next month, and official telephone service will be available in September. Trial calls between Nanjing and Shanghai were made the day before yesterday, and the sound quality was very clear. Before the Ministry of Communications sets the rates, long-distance call fees will be charged according to existing rates.
