French Water and Electricity Company

Disguised Price Increase for Water and Electricity 153

Citizens request disapproval.

The Second District Branch of the Citizens' United Association of the Second Special District sent a letter to the Board of Directors of the French Concession, which reads: "We hereby inform you that we have received a joint letter from various businesses on the Avenue Edward VII, stating that businesses have been affected by the economic downturn in recent years, the market is sluggish, and business is poor. Closures due to inability to sustain operations are heard of daily. Unexpectedly, at this time when there is no avenue for appeal, we suddenly received a notice in French from the French Water and Electricity Company, stating that starting in July, fees for water and electricity meter installation and deposits would be increased. Upon reading this, we were extremely surprised. Water and electricity are public utilities, and their main purpose is to serve the convenience of the citizens, not like other businesses that can be greedy and insatiable. Moreover, in this time of commercial hardship, water and electricity companies are still making profits of over one million yuan annually, yet they are still not satisfied. They disregard the suffering of the citizens and arbitrarily increase prices in a disguised manner, which is unreasonable and unjust. The Board of Directors of the French Concession, at this time of extreme economic panic and when citizens are feeling extremely burdened, has failed to observe the public sentiment and has rashly approved this increase, which is a disservice to the spirit of cooperation between the authorities and the people. We feel particularly regretful. Businesses are determined not to recognize this unreasonable price increase for water and electricity. We have always admired your association as an organization that seeks welfare for the citizens. Therefore, we are submitting this report and requesting that your association send a letter to the Board of Directors of the French Concession, argue based on reason, and demand the cancellation of this resolution. We will not stop until our goal is achieved, and we pledge our full support. We hope you will not back down even slightly, and we will be extremely grateful." In response to this, after investigation, water and electricity are public utilities, and all actions should be based on the welfare of the citizens. Now, in this time of rural bankruptcy, economic downturn, and the decline of all industries, the French Water and Electricity Company is implementing this disguised price increase, which violates public opinion and disregards the suffering of the citizens, which is highly objectionable. Therefore, we are sending this letter on behalf of the citizens and requesting that your bureau consider the difficulties of the times, uphold the spirit of cooperation, and consider the suffering of the citizens. Please promptly revoke the approval of this unreasonable price increase to avoid causing resentment among the citizens and creating unnecessary disputes. We hope you will investigate.

Security Department

Resolution of the Dispute Over the Purchase of Rice by a Cook 155

Squad leader Qian Jihua is being strictly investigated. Platoon leader Bu Wenbin has been demoted. The Heshang Rice Store on Dayang Bridge in Zhabei and the Second Platoon of the Second Regiment of the Security Department had a dispute over the purchase of rice, which led to a strike. After the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce, together with representatives from all sectors of Zhabei, persuaded them to resume business, the Municipal Security Department also investigated the matter and imposed punishments. The details are as follows:

Handling Measures 156

The Municipal Security Department sent a letter to the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce yesterday, which reads: "We have received your Chamber's official letters No. 15, 17, and 23, regarding the case of the dispute between the Heshang Rice Store on Dayang Bridge and the Second Platoon of our Department's Second Regiment over the purchase of rice. You requested that we investigate and severely punish the parties involved in order to maintain commerce and reassure the people. We have approved this request. After investigating this case, our department received reports from the Second Regiment and complaints from the Heshang Rice Store. We directly dispatched personnel to conduct a thorough investigation and submit a factual report. After considering all the circumstances and making a fair judgment, we have determined that Squad Leader Qian Jihua acted without authorization and violated military discipline, and deserves punishment. The rice store did not follow proper business practices and rashly provoked the dispute, and is also at fault and cannot evade responsibility. On the 9th of this month, Zhang Lianyu, a cook from the Second Platoon, purchased two dou of rice from the rice store and asked the Sen Tai Store, where they usually deposit dough, to weigh it for him. He found that it was short by twelve liang. The cook took the rice back to the rice store to request compensation. The rice store, accustomed to disrespecting small customers, arrogantly insulted him, poured the rice into a bucket, threw back the payment, and verbally abused the cook. The cook, feeling wronged, returned to the platoon to report the incident. The soldiers were outraged by the arrogance of the rice store. Chen Zhichao, the duty platoon leader, did not fully believe the cook's one-sided account and ordered the duty squad leader, Qian Jihua, to invite the store owner to the platoon to inquire about the situation in order to ascertain the truth. However, the store owner refused to go, and the squad leader resorted to coercion, resulting in a physical altercation. Jiang Dianle, the patrol officer of the Fourth District, arrived after hearing the news to mediate. Bu Wenbin, the platoon leader of the platoon, also returned to the platoon from outside at that time and immediately apologized to the patrol officer and the rice store owner, and offered them tea and water before leaving. He then reprimanded the squad leader for violating the duty platoon leader's order to invite the store owner to the platoon to ask questions peacefully, and abusing his authority. The squad leader was detained pending further action. This is the actual situation of the incident on that day, which our department has investigated several times and found to be true. The rice store's shortage of weight can be proven by the signed statement of Jin Gensheng, the owner of the Sen Tai Store who weighed the rice for the cook. Platoon Leader Bu Wenbin's apology and hospitality to the rice store owner was witnessed by Patrol Officer Jiang Dianle. In all fairness, Squad Leader Qian Jihua acted beyond his authority and deserves to be condemned. The rice store's unfair transaction led to the incident, and both parties are unfortunate, which our department deeply regrets. Our department has always regarded merchants and soldiers as one, and military discipline is especially strict. Any soldier who commits a fault will be punished to the fullest extent of the law, and we will never tolerate any misconduct. We have now reported to the Municipal Government and will transfer the squad leader to our department for strict investigation and punishment in accordance with military law. As for Platoon Leader Bu Wenbin, his handling of the situation at the time was not inappropriate. However, the actions of his soldiers dared to exceed the scope of his orders. He is responsible for his usual neglect of education and cannot escape blame. He is hereby demoted to lieutenant as a minor punishment and will be retained in his original position to observe his future performance. In conclusion, harmony and goodwill should be the main principles between the military and the people. Our department will learn from the past and be wary of the future, and will strictly restrain our subordinates. Any offense will be punished. We also hope that merchants and the people will respect public morals and conduct fair transactions, so that all grievances can be eliminated and everyone can live in peace."

Chamber of Commerce's Attitude 157

In addition to sending a letter to the Chamber of Commerce regarding the handling of the case, the Municipal Security Department also sent Secretary Hou Dachun to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to explain the details of the investigation and discuss solutions. He was received by Secretary Yan Ersheng of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce. After discussions, both parties expressed their willingness to handle the case fairly. The Chamber of Commerce believed that the Security Department's punishment of Duty Squad Leader Qian Jihua and the demotion of Platoon Leader Bu Wenbin showed Director Yang's concern for commerce and impartiality. The Chamber of Commerce will persuade the merchants and people in the area to understand the situation and ensure peaceful transactions in the future to eliminate all grievances. It is reported that the Municipal Chamber of Commerce will send a letter to the representatives of the merchants and people in the area, inviting them to the meeting this morning to explain everything.

Ministry of Finance Approves Chamber of Commerce Request

Extend the Validity Period of National Seafood Permits 159

Whether imported or domestic, the validity period is one year. The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce previously received a letter from the Shanghai Seafood and Groceries Trade Association, stating that the validity period of permits for domestic razor clams, wood ear mushrooms, shiitake mushrooms, dried shrimp, and other items was shorter than that of imported goods, hindering transportation and sales. The Chamber telegraphed the Ministry of Finance requesting that the validity period be the same as that of imported goods, i.e., one year. It has now been learned that the Ministry of Finance approved the Chamber's request yesterday, allowing the validity period to be the same as that of imported goods. The original text is as follows: "We have received your telegram and have instructed the Inspector General of Customs to instruct the Jianghai Customs to investigate. All razor clams, wood ear mushrooms, shiitake mushrooms, dried shrimp, and other items are regarded by the Customs as items that cannot be stored for too long. Whether imported or domestic, the validity period of the permits used is set at less than one year. Now, considering the business situation, the Jianghai Customs has revised the validity period of permits for razor clams and other items to one year to facilitate transportation and sales. Please inform them."

Chamber of Commerce Letter to the Finance Bureau

Request to Postpone the Increase in Tobacco and Alcohol License Tax 160

Collect according to the amount handled by the Ministry

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce received a petition from over fifty representatives, including Chen Liangyu of the Shanghai Tobacco Exchange Trade Association, Zhu Liwu of the Restaurant Trade Association, Lan Qinghe of the Sauce and Wine Store Association, Li Bingen of the Western Tobacco Trade Association, and Yang Qiaosheng and Liao Zhongwen of the Fen Wine Trade Association, stating that after the license tax was transferred to the city's administration, the increased tax amount was unbearable. They specifically went to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to petition and forward the petition to the mayor, ordering a postponement of the tax increase to avoid disputes, etc. The chairman of the Chamber, Yu Zuoting, and Secretary Yan Ersheng, received the petition, as reported in yesterday's newspaper. It is now learned that the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce sent a letter to the Municipal Finance Bureau yesterday, requesting a temporary postponement of the tax increase and to collect according to the amount handled by the Ministry. The original text is as follows: (Omitted above) "Although the Provisional Regulations on Tobacco and Alcohol Business Licenses were promulgated by the Ministry in the twentieth year of the Republic of China, merchants and people have been requesting amendments to them to this day. Therefore, when the Ministry handled it, it took into account the facts and did not collect the full amount according to the regulations, which can be proven by the facts. Since the Shanghai business market has experienced the anti-Japanese war and the world economic recession, it has been in a state of decline. In particular, the tobacco exchange industry is known as the "husband and wife shop," and it is difficult to compare it with ordinary stores. When the Ministry handled it, it took into account the difficulties of the merchants. Since it is now handled by the city, it is better to increase the actual revenue than before, which is not the way to benefit merchants and the people. Moreover, the reform of the tobacco and alcohol license tax to local control was originally intended to compensate for the harsh and miscellaneous taxes. Since there are no harsh and miscellaneous taxes that can be cut in this city, it is purely an increase in revenue rather than compensation. It is even more possible to collect according to the number of collections handled by the Ministry to promote tolerance. According to the letter's previous situation, we hereby request that your bureau investigate and approve that it still be handled according to the old precedent, with the old exchanged for the new, which is indeed a public friendship."

Retrial Record of the Liu Chongwu Case 166

Liu and others did not admit to premeditated murder. The prosecutor asked the presiding judge to leniently sentence. In the winter of the year before last, the Maotai Foreign Goods Store on Xinzha Road, the Yuheng Foreign Goods Store on Hankou Road, the Sunkwang Hing Clock Store on Henan Road, as well as Maotai, Xinmingxing, and other foreign goods stores, were selling inferior goods. Original Verdict Was Reversed 167

Liu, Pan, and Cao were each sentenced to twelve years of imprisonment, and Tian Shuiyang was sentenced to six years. Liu and others were also dissatisfied and appealed to the Supreme Court. The groups in this city also felt that Liu and others were subject to legal punishment because of sanctions against traitors, which made the patriotic movement feel cold, so they appealed everywhere to try to rescue them. Liu and others did not admit to the crime of premeditated murder, saying that the purpose of going to the stores at that time was to warn the traitors, and there was no intention of killing or injuring people. Municipal Chamber of Commerce Advocates

Improving Chinese Bookkeeping 171

The joint training course is now open for registration. The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce and accountant Xu Yongzuo have strongly promoted the movement to improve Chinese bookkeeping in recent years. Last December, the Chamber of Commerce held a large-scale lecture and exhibition, which set a new record for attendance and viewership. Recently, there are plans to jointly organize an improved Chinese bookkeeping training course. It is reported that this plan has become concrete and that registration will be open simultaneously at the Chamber of Commerce and Xu Accountant Firm starting today. All matters concerning education and training will be jointly overseen by accountant Xu Yongzuo and Yan Esheng, the president of a commercial school. The rationale and detailed rules of the improved Chinese bookkeeping training course are recorded below:

Rationale: The current bookkeeping methods in our country can be broadly divided into Chinese and Western styles. Western bookkeeping uses horizontal registration, relying on imported paper and ink, and the accounting principles and methods are rigidly adhering to Western practices. Not only is it difficult to imitate, but it is also very costly. Chinese bookkeeping uses vertical recording, with paper and ink all being domestic goods. The accounting principles and methods are familiar to Chinese people. However, the system is not perfect and lacks organization, which is not aligned with the purpose of accounting. Therefore, it is also criticized. I, as an accountant, have served the community for many years and have been concerned about the inadequacies of the current bookkeeping system. I have launched a movement to improve Chinese bookkeeping, giving lectures at various universities and writing articles in various magazines, advocating for improving Chinese bookkeeping based on our country's inherent system and adopting the latest world academic principles, using the most economical and effective methods. The news spread, which has aroused the sympathy of the academic and business circles. Since last year, after publishing a special book with concrete plans and explanations for improving Chinese bookkeeping, it has aroused the attention of the entire society, and discussions and adoption have been widespread. It can be seen that improving Chinese bookkeeping has gone from advocacy to implementation. Last winter, the Chamber of Commerce, in view of the importance of improved Chinese bookkeeping, held a large-scale exhibition and lecture, publicly exhibiting the ledgers, books, charts, and tables of improved Chinese bookkeeping. I, the accountant, also attended and lectured, and tens of thousands of attendees praised it. At that time, the audience requested more detailed lectures and the establishment of a special training class for long-term study. However, due to busy duties, it has not been possible to hold it. In the past year, the adoption of improved Chinese bookkeeping has become increasingly popular, and the effectiveness has become increasingly apparent, and requests to open training courses have become more frequent. From far away, such as Shaanxi, Sichuan, Guangdong, Guangxi, and the South Seas Islands, and nearby, such as Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Shandong, Jiangxi, and Anhui, letters are often received requesting correspondence courses. This shows that improving bookkeeping is universally supported, and opening a training class cannot be delayed any longer. Therefore, the Chamber of Commerce and I, the accountant, have jointly formulated regulations to hold a large-scale training course to teach the accounting principles and methods of improved Chinese bookkeeping. Every morning, during spare time, a one-hour lecture will be held at the Chamber of Commerce's assembly hall, adopting strict training, and charging a very small fee, with the aim of completing the study in two months, ensuring that students can obtain a comprehensive understanding and skills of improved Chinese bookkeeping after graduation, and serve the community, being able to perform their duties with ease. All accounting personnel of companies and firms, or those who aspire to study improved Chinese bookkeeping, regardless of gender or age, can apply for admission according to the admission requirements. Companies and firms that need to train their accounting personnel to improve their bookkeeping can also send them to study, which is an excellent opportunity to study improved Chinese bookkeeping. Do not miss this opportunity.

Detailed Rules:

1. Name: This training course is jointly organized by the Commercial School of the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce and the Accounting Tutorial School of Accountant Xu Yongzuo. It is named the Improved Chinese Bookkeeping Training Course.

2. Purpose: The purpose of this training course is to cultivate talents in improved Chinese bookkeeping.

3. Subject: The subject of this training course is to teach the accounting principles and methods of improved Chinese bookkeeping.

4. Teaching Time: One hour of instruction every day except Sunday, from 7:40 AM to 8:40 AM.

5. Duration: From August 1st to September 29th.

6. Admission Requirements: No age limit, no gender discrimination. Anyone with clear writing and reasoning skills and some accounting experience may apply for admission.

7. Registration: Registration is open at any time before July 30th. A registration fee of one yuan and two 2.5-inch half-length photos must be submitted. Those who are not admitted will have their photos returned with a receipt.

8. Admission Examination: An interview will be conducted during registration to assess Chinese language and arithmetic skills. However, those who can provide a letter of proof from a trade association or company stating that they have clear writing and reasoning skills and accounting experience may be exempted from the examination.

9. Admission Procedures: Fill out an application form and pay all the required fees before admission.

10. Fees: Each person must pay the following fees: Tuition fee of two yuan, lecture notes and practical exercise book fee of two yuan.

11. Withdrawal: There will be no refunds for any fees paid for withdrawals made mid-course.

12. Certificate of Completion: Upon completion of the course with satisfactory grades, a graduation certificate will be issued by the training course.

13. Address: Classroom: Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce Assembly Hall. Registration Office: Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce Commercial School (Address: Tianhou Palace Bridge, Henan Road, Shanghai), Xu Yongzuo Accountant Firm Accounting Tutorial School (Address: 160 Avenue Edward VII, Shanghai).

14. Supplementary Provisions: This training course reserves the right to amend these rules at any time if there are any unaddressed matters.

It Rained Again Yesterday in This City

The Weather Turned Cooler After a Short Time 172

The weather in this city has been very dry. Although the two rains on the afternoon and evening of the day before yesterday (the 17th) did not help agricultural work at all, the weather has turned slightly cooler. Starting yesterday morning, the sky was covered with dark clouds, indicating that it would continue to rain. As expected, at about 8 o'clock, the overcast sky closed in, with intermittent showers. However, it stopped after about ten minutes, with the rainfall being heavier near Nanshi, while only a few drops fell in Zhabei. At about 1:30 PM, there was another drizzle, which lasted for about ten minutes. At about 2 o'clock, it rained again, although the raindrops were slightly larger than before, it also stopped after only ten minutes. Afterwards, there was a cool breeze, which refreshed the mind. Compared with the temperature more than ten days ago, it was like heaven and earth.

The Weather Is Unseasonal

The Number of Epidemic Patients Has Increased Sharply 173

There is also the possibility of finding true cholera. The heat in this city has decreased after the rain seen on the current day (the 17th), but the rainfall time was very short and the amount of rain was especially scarce. On the rural side, the benefit is very shallow. Although it still rained from time to time yesterday, due to the sudden rain and sunshine, the nitrogenous climate has changed drastically, and the ground emits a turbid smell that makes people want to vomit. As a result, the epidemic has increased sharply. A Datong News Agency reporter visited the emergency epidemic hospital on North Xizang Road last night and learned from the female doctor Qin Meixian of the hospital that 58 patients were admitted from morning to dusk yesterday, all suffering from gastroenteritis, which is the highest record since the hospital opened. If the weather remains unstable, there is a possibility that true cholera may be discovered, she said. Now we will explore the number of outpatients in the hospital since it opened on the 9th of this month.

The total number of outpatients is 841, and the number of inpatients is 364. An ambulance is dispatched every day to patrol various places in Zhabei. When a patient is found, they are immediately carried onto the ambulance and sent to the hospital for emergency treatment. Therefore, the hospital's protection of epidemic patients is meticulous.

A Worker Was Frightened by Gunfire

Fell into the River and Drowned 174

The foreman filed a lawsuit against the security team members, and the district court opened the trial to investigate. Coal workers at the Baotai Silk Factory in Xicaoge Temple, Longhua Town, had a dispute over work on the afternoon of June 8. The Ninth District Party Headquarters there heard about it and, fearing a major disaster, immediately notified the Longhua Town Security Team. Team leader Wu Shougang ordered team members Tang Zuxian, Wu Fusheng, Wu Yinxiang, Hu Youcai, etc., to go to suppress the dispute. Unexpectedly, the team members encountered the workers on the way, and it is unknown how they caused trouble for the security team members. The team members, for the sake of self-defense, fired several shots into the sky to get rid of the workers. After the incident, foreman Hu Yude filed a complaint with the prosecutor's office of the District Court against the security team members for firing guns, stating that worker Qi Desheng was carrying coal and was suddenly frightened by the gunfire and fell into the river and drowned, and that his body was missing, etc., and named Lan Yongqing, who was carrying the coal with Qi Desheng, as a witness. Prosecutor Wu Derong ordered an investigation with a thousand witnesses, and at the end of the investigation, a public prosecution was filed, stating that the defendants should be prosecuted for the murder case, and listing the facts of the defendants' crimes, the reasons for the prosecution, and the criminal provisions. The reason for this is that Wu Shoukang, Tang Liangen, and Ji Xiaomao (that is, Ji Wenbin) knew each other. At 2:00 PM on June 8, Tang Liangen

Hu Yude quarreled over contracting coal carrying, and Wu Shoukang sent team members Wu Youcai, Wu Yinxiang, Tang Zuxian, Wu Fusheng, etc. to arrest Hu Yude's workers and threaten them with guns. At that time, Song Yongqing and Qi Desheng were carrying coal on their shoulders and were on the springboard when they were frightened by the sound of gunfire and fell into the water. Qi Desheng drowned and disappeared. The reason for Hu Yude's lawsuit is that the facts mentioned above in the prosecution and the criminal provisions were interrogated by Wu Shoukang, Tang Liangen, and Ji Xiaomao, who denied the allegations. However, Hu Yude and Song Yongqing clearly stated the details, and Wang Qishan, Wang Fushan, and Mao Chunfu also testified that they did hear Hu Yude's workers being frightened by the gunfire and falling into the water, and that they were not rescued. Wu Shoukang also did not deny sending team members to threaten with guns. It is obvious that the statements of Wu Shoukang, Tang Liangen, and Ji Xiaomao are sophistry. Wu Shoukang, Tang Liangen, Ji Xiaomao, Wu Youcai, Wu Yinxiang, Tang Zuxian, and Wu Fusheng clearly committed the crime under Article 291 of the Criminal Law, etc. The day before yesterday, Judge Zhang Peiming opened the trial. The defendants hired lawyers Pan Zhensheng and Zhu Fang to appear in court to defend them. According to Hu Yude, he is from Shanyang, and the deceased, Kai Desheng, still has an uncle in his hometown. Except for Wu Yinxiang, who did not arrive due to illness, the defendants all arrived as summoned. According to Wu Shoukang, he was notified by the Shanxi Party Headquarters to send personnel to suppress the dispute. However, an investigation revealed that no one had fallen into the water and drowned. The judge stated that the case was important and that there was a need for further investigation, and that the trial would continue.

Ping Pong Dispute Lawsuit

The Trial Was Concluded Yesterday and Sentencing Is Scheduled 175

The China Jiande Association table tennis team suffered great damage to its reputation due to illegal refereeing by the Xiangbin Cup table tennis tournament organizing committee, and filed a lawsuit with the First Special Court requesting confirmation that the illegal verdict was invalid. The details have been recorded in this newspaper. Yesterday morning, Judge Zhang Qinglan of the First Special Court opened a hearing, and the plaintiff Lu Xiu lawyer, accompanied by the lawyers Yang Ruinian, E Sen, and Yin Jingxian, and the defendant Zhi Lu Xi Niao, accompanied by lawyers Jiang Yiping and Wu Baotai, appeared in court. First, Lu Xiu lawyer stated that he was the captain of the Jiande table tennis team. The team participated in the Xiangbin Cup table tennis tournament hosted by the defendant, and the result was that the team and the Guangdong team each scored 17 points. The defendant then set the final on May 19 at the Meifeng table tennis room, but on the 19th, the team suddenly received a letter from the defendant, notifying them of a change of date. The reason was that the Guangdong team believed that the venue was too small and requested a change of date. Although the team was fully prepared, they had to comply and not go. Subsequently, the period for the selection of Chinese athletes to prepare for the Far East Games with the Japanese team was combined. The team participated because of the great significance and honor of winning glory for the country. The Whole Story of the Plotting and Rioting of Bandits in Pudong

Zhu Alan's Various Crimes Zhu Shaoqing Was Originally a Military Advisor. The case of the robbers occurring in the area of Lujiada Bridge in the west of Zhangjiang Wang Town, Pudong, resulting in the death of the escorted bandit Zhu Alan, was briefly reported in yesterday's newspaper. Now we will explore the detailed circumstances of the case and continue to record them as follows. First of all, the bandit Zhu Alan was a native of Qinjia Town in the Fourth District of Nanhui. He had been associated with bandits and was sentenced to 12 years in prison by the county government for illegally possessing military fire in the years 7 and 8 of the Republic of China. During the time of Sun Chuanfang's army's arrival in Shanghai, he took the opportunity to escape. In the 13th year of the Republic of China, he ganged up with Hong Xiangtao and others to destroy the Western Bridge at No. 31 Huhan Road to plot trouble. Later, Hong Xiangtao was sentenced to death, while Zhu escaped without a trace. In the 14th year of the Republic of China, he robbed the home of Xu Zhuchun in the east of Qinjia Town. In the spring of the 16th year, he raped Tang Wu, a resident of Qinjia Town, and severely beat her husband Tang Chatao, causing permanent disability. Mr. Tang is still alive today,

And Hates Them Deeply. 176

In the 17th year of the Republic of China, he ganged up to kidnap the old mother of Chen Deyi near Chenjiahang, Shanghai County, and was sentenced to imprisonment again. In the 18th year of the Republic of China, Wang Boxiang's house in Luotuo Temple was robbed twice, all under his instigation. In the 20th year of the Republic of China, although Zhu escaped in the case of the robbery of Lin Linquan's home in Linjiaquan, his henchman Tang Jincai is still in prison. In the 22nd year of the Republic of China, he instigated the robbery of Zhang Agui's home in Xisong Bridge. In summary, the bandit has committed countless crimes throughout his life. However, most of the victims dare not speak out because his party members are fierce and for the sake of their own livelihoods. Although he has been sentenced to imprisonment several times, he has always relied on his capable henchmen and made every effort to rescue him, avoiding death. In the summer of this year, Nanhui County Magistrate Yuan Xiluo received a secret report stating that Zhu Alan had opened a teahouse, gathered scum, sold prohibited drugs, and colluded with the communists to

Transfer Military Fire, 177

etc., and secretly ordered the Zhangjiang Fence Public Security Bureau to arrest him within a time limit. After receiving the order, Director Sun of the Branch Bureau dispatched officers to track him down day and night, and finally intercepted him on the afternoon of the 16th in the Sanjieqiao area near Beicai. He immediately found suspicious letters on his person and detained him at the fence. After a preliminary interrogation, his language was cunning and he firmly denied the allegations. Therefore, on the evening of the 17th, he dispatched Inspector Gan and a police officer, and also requested two members from the security team for assistance. He also hired a net boat in advance, because the weather was dry and the water was shallow, and the inland river could not carry passengers. He instructed them to drive the empty boat to Lujiada Bridge and wait. Because the bandit had many henchmen and was afraid of being noticed, he escorted the bandit Zhu Alan at about 10 o'clock in the evening, armed with four team police, intending to take the boat at Lujiada Bridge. He was familiar with the road and arrived a few hundred steps away from Lujiada Bridge. Dozens of gunshots suddenly rang out in the nearby fields. The two team members were startled and

Fell to the Ground and Fired Back. 178

The gunfire from the other side suddenly became dense. The bandit Zhu Alan suddenly broke free, turned around and tried to snatch the firearm from the inspector's hand, and shouted loudly, intending to meet the other side. The patrolman blew his whistle madly and ran back to report. The escorting team police fired their guns to resist, repelling the would-be robbers. For a moment, bullets rained down, and the bandit Zhu Alan was shot dead by stray bullets. The town police were on their way out to defend when they received the report and immediately went to assist, tracking down the robbers in all directions, but they had all disappeared far away. They then returned to defend in different directions and did not leave all night. The merchants and residents of the entire town and the nearby villagers were all extremely frightened. The district team bureau urgently reported to the county government after the incident

To Verify the Bandit's Corpse. 179

And at noon on the 18th, gathered all the town police, together with the local villager Deputy Shen Shaoshan, went to Qin Town Bandit's Nest to search for the remaining bandits. He arrested Zhu Shaoqing, Zhu Alan's brother, in the teahouse, and found letters, bullets, and other items in his home. He was over half a hundred years old and resourceful. Most of the cases Zhu Alan committed were his schemes, so the bandits regarded him as a military advisor. It is now reported that the Public Security Branch Bureau, in view of the previous case, intends to request the county government to send a water patrol team to the district to take custody of the suspect, and on the other hand, order each jia to continue special martial law from the night of the 18th to prevent any further accidents.

Price Increase for Chinese Public Buses 182

Due to the drastic drop in the exchange rate of copper coins and the rise in gasoline prices on the 22nd of this month, the public transportation industry in the city has suffered greatly. Electric vehicles in the concessions have already increased their prices. The Zhabei Chinese Public Bus Company has also been affected by the depreciation of copper coins, and it is said that the monthly deficit is more than 4,000 yuan. Therefore, it applied to the authorities for an increase in fares to maintain operations. It has now been approved and will be implemented on the 22nd of this month. Except for the special bus from North Station to Jinan University on Route 3, the fare for the entire line remains unchanged at 20 cents. For the remaining buses, one copper coin will be added for the first and second stops, and two copper coins will be added for each stop starting from the third stop. The new price list is as follows: Route 1: 9 to 35 copper coins for the entire line; Route 3: 9 to 50 copper coins; Route 4: 9 to 47 copper coins from North Station to the Municipal Government (North Neilu); The extended section of the Municipal Government to the Municipal Government Staff Dormitory is a temporary operation, and the fare remains at 12 copper coins.

Public Works Department

Health Report for June 184

The Director of the Health Department of the Public Works Department reported for the month of June, "Except for the lack of rain, the weather was generally normal this month. However, starting on the 25th, it suddenly turned very hot. Fortunately, the transmission of Liang disease did not increase as a result. There were only 6,000 cases of heatstroke, and the number of deaths was not high.

Increased Work 185

Due to the arrival of the hot season, the workload of the Health Department has increased, especially the management of retail cold drinks, which is difficult. Among them, many are unreliable. The enforcement work of the Health Department will be effective if it receives the cooperation and attention of the public. However, diseases caused by cold drinks have not been seen much. However, there are more patients with typhoid fever, which may be related to this.

Key Points for Disease Prevention 186

The public should pay more attention to whether their own kitchens, basements, and toilets are clean in the summer. The key to preventing disease is to be careful with food. Although this is a very trivial matter, one must not shirk the labor. Also, if servants are sick, one should pay close attention to them, lest they spread it to the whole family.

Well Disinfection 187

Cholera was not found in June. However, disinfectants were placed in the wells as usual. The Waterworks Company has agreed to provide free water in the poor areas, which has been implemented since June 28th. Recently, many residents near the water wells have volunteered to disinfect them, so the personnel performing the task can use this to know the location of the wells. This change in attitude is a very gratifying thing.

Cholera Prevention 188

Cholera prevention work is proceeding as usual. Because the Municipal Government is holding the 13th Health and Cleaning Movement, the Health Department is cooperating and stepping up publicity. A total of 55,299 people were injected this month. In terms of population, this number seems too small. However, those who are injected are all voluntary, and the general habit of people is not to take preventive measures until after the infection has been discovered. However, it is often too late.

Comparison of Births and Deaths 189

The number of bathers in outdoor swimming pools reached 18,279, which is almost double that of June last year. Therefore, the number of supervisors had to be increased. This month's population births, as reported, were 51 foreigners and 193 Chinese. The mortality rate was 10.94 per thousand for foreigners and 12.81 per thousand for Chinese, which are both quite low compared to the historical average for June.

Major Factories in This City

Benefit from Using Domestic Glycerin 191

The Xingqiu (Planet) brand glycerin, created by Chinese people, is of excellent quality and reasonably priced. Since the lifting of tariffs, its sales have been very prosperous. Many local factories, such as China Chemical, Family, Yonghe, Meixing, Xianshi, Nanyang, and Hua, have all purchased and used it extensively. Since the price of glycerin from Europe and the United States has increased, and import taxes have been added, if Shanghai did not have domestically produced glycerin, foreign goods would have already risen in price. The factories that need glycerin would inevitably be affected. The close relationship between raw materials and finished products means that our country has traditionally lacked raw materials, leading to high production costs. As a result, our goods often cannot compete with foreign goods in the market. It is not easy for domestically produced glycerin to achieve such success. It is hoped that major industrialists at home and abroad will continue to promote it, so that both parties can benefit.

China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Investigates the Jiangtian Steamer 192

Collision with the Huguang Sand Lightship 193

The Jianghan Customs has sent a letter to the head office to thoroughly investigate the truth of the accident. The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Yangtze River steamer, the Jiangtian, which was traveling from Beijing to Wuhan, damaged a lightship set up by the Jianghan Customs upstream. The Customs is now seeking compensation from the company. The company has not received a detailed report and cannot assess the situation. It has ordered the owner of the steamer to promptly report the actual situation. The circumstances are described below:

Cause of the Lightship Collision 194

The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's old Yangtze River steamer has been chartered by the central government. It was recently renovated and sent to the capital for official duties. On the 7th of this month, the steamer sailed upstream to Wuhan. When it reached the Huguang Sand lightship area near Hankou, the Jianghan Customs had set up a lightship there to warn Yangtze River steamers of navigational safety, displaying signs to prevent merchant ships from running aground and causing accidents. As the Jiangtian steamer sailed through the Huguang Sand area, due to the strong winds and turbulent tides, the hull was subjected to wind and wave pressure, causing it to collide with the Customs lightship, damaging its hull.

Customs Demands Compensation 195

After the incident occurred, the Jianghan Customs river patrol investigated and reported the extent of the damage to the Huguang Sand lightship and the circumstances of the Jiangtian steamer's accident to the port authority. They contacted the owner of the Jiangtian steamer to demand compensation for the loss. At the same time, they sent a letter to the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, requesting compensation for the loss of the Huguang Sand lightship, and urgently sent workers to carry out major repairs to avoid hindering the navigation of other ships.

Order to the Ship Owner to Report Quickly 196

Yesterday, the Shanghai China Merchants Steam Navigation Company received this letter, along with a report from the owner of the Jiangtian steamer stating that the Jiangtian steamer was subjected to wind and water pressure when passing through Huguang Sand, and collided with the lightship. At that time, it safely passed through. According to the report from the officer on duty, the lightship was not heard to sound an alarm indicating that it had been severely damaged. The company believed that the ship owner's report did not indicate any major damage, which did not match the river patrol's report. Therefore, yesterday, the company issued an order to the Jiangtian ship owner, Qin Lin, to quickly submit a detailed report on the damage to the Huguang Sand lightship and the extent of the damage to the lightship for verification.

Installation of Light Buoys Near Sunken Ship Destroyed 204

Hydrographic Bureau of the Ministry of the Navy Navigation Notice No. 92: A light buoy has been installed in the "Yuanyuansha" channel south of the Yangtze River estuary on the east coast of the Republic of China, and the sunken ship nearby has been destroyed. Navigation Notice No. 118 of the 21st year of the Republic of China should be repealed. Position: 101 degrees north of the "Jiudu Xiaota" lighthouse in the South Channel, a distance of 2.32 nautical miles, i.e., approximately 121 degrees 42 minutes east longitude and 31 degrees 19 minutes north latitude. Explanation: The sunken ship has now been destroyed, and the symbol should be removed from the charts. Related charts: Navy Chart No. 505. Issuing agency: Hydrographic Bureau of the Ministry of the Navy. Note: The directions in this navigation notice are calculated using true north as 0 degrees, turning to the right to 359 degrees. However, the direction of the light is calculated from the sea. The luminous power is based on clear weather. Fog signals are only used in foggy weather. Depth records are calculated according to the datum plane used in the largest scale chart and will be explained separately if necessary. July 10, 23rd year of the Republic of China.

Reading Questions and Answers

Regarding "An Outline of Literature" (Continued) 223

Reply to Zhou Yun Jun

We can divide the questions raised by Mr. Zhou into three parts to answer: First, what should an outline of literature provide to readers? Second, is Pan's "Outline of Literature" good or not? Third, which outline of literature is more readable?

An outline of literature, as the name suggests, is a summarized account of various issues in the field of literature, making it easier for beginners to grasp a simple and clear concept of literature and thus know how to study literature. This is not a compilation, nor does it become a monograph, because a compilation is only putting together the opinions of various schools and individuals, without the need to add one's own opinions. However, writing an outline of literature cannot be done this way. It requires the author to have a fixed literary stance and a systematic theoretical study; otherwise, readers will feel clueless and the content will seem disorganized. For example, when discussing the definition of literature, you can certainly cite various different opinions such as those of Oscar Wilde, Taine, Tolstoy, and Mikhailovsky, but you must not forget the era you are in and your own views. You must have crucial annotations for those different opinions, so that readers can understand which ones are right and which ones are wrong, without feeling confused. Also, an outline cannot emphasize one issue too much or ignore another. It needs to take all aspects into account (of course, your own opinions are still necessary). For example, when discussing the evolution of literature, you should not only talk about Aestheticism or completely dismiss Aestheticism. You must briefly discuss everything from Classicism to Socialist Realism. The content of an outline should not be too empty or too complicated. Rather than being all-encompassing and turning it into a mess, it is better to be simple and able to grasp the core of the theory. An outline of literature is written for beginners in literature or those who do not necessarily specialize in literature but only need to acquire some basic literary knowledge.

From the reader's perspective, one should not have excessive expectations when reading an outline of literature. The main purpose is only to solve some simple questions such as what is literature and the essence of literature. If you think that an outline should be all-encompassing and that you should know everything about literature after reading one, then you are exaggerating yourself. An outline can only give you a correct hint on each issue. What happens after the hint is given is further research, which is not the responsibility of the outline. To criticize whether an outline is good or not, the first thing to consider is whether the book is systematic, whether the theory is correct, and whether it points us in the right direction. As for Mr. Zhou's feeling of emptiness, I am afraid it is because Mr. Zhou is a little too demanding of the outline of literature.

Free Talk

Water Nature 224

— Gong Han

The weather has been extremely hot for nearly twenty days. Looking at the Shanghai newspapers, almost every day there are records of people drowning while swimming in the river. This is rare in our village.

Our village has a lot of water, and people have a lot of knowledge about water and many can float. If you can't float, you don't go into the water easily. This ability to float is commonly called "knowing water nature."

This "knowing water nature," if explained in more detail using the "comprador" vernacular, is: first, knowing that fire can burn people to death, and water can also drown people, but water looks gentle and seems easy to approach, so it is also easy to be fooled; second, knowing that although water can drown people, it can also float people, so now we try to manipulate it, specifically to use its ability to float people; third, is learning the manipulation method. Once this method is mastered, "knowing water nature" is considered complete.

But people in the city not only cannot float, but also seem to have forgotten that water can drown people. They are not prepared at all, and they don't even measure the depth of the water before jumping in when it gets unbearably hot. If they unfortunately end up in a deep spot, then of course they will die. And I feel that people in the city who are willing to try to help seem to be fewer than in the countryside.

But saving city people is probably more difficult, because not only must the rescuer "know water nature," but the rescued person must also "know water nature" to some extent. He should not use any force, and let the rescuer hold his chin and float him to a shallow place. If he is too impatient and desperately climbs onto the rescuer, then if the rescuer is not skilled, he will have to sink with him.

So I think, if you want to go into the river, it is best to learn a little floating skills beforehand, and you don't have to go to a swimming pool in a park, just go to the riverside, but you must have an expert to guide you. Secondly, if for various reasons you can't learn to float, then use a bamboo pole to probe the depth of the river water first, and just dabble in the shallow water, or the safest thing to do is to scoop up the water and just rinse yourself on the river bank. And the most important thing is to know that water has the nature of drowning people who can't swim, and you must remember it firmly!

Now, advocating the promotion of such common sense may seem crazy, or aimed at "gossip," but the facts prove that this is definitely not the case. Many things cannot be done with our eyes closed, just to please progressive critics.

Summer Travel 225

— Liu Ming

(1)

On a summer morning, people who are tired of living in the city only need to be on the train and see the green rice fields covered in thin mist, the cotton fields with lemon-yellow flowers, and the families with one or two black buffaloes tied in front of their doors to feel refreshed. Moreover, at the final destination, they are greeted by the sea dotted with tea-brown sails and the mixed sea breeze that brushes against their clothes.

Summer is really a season that tempts people to travel!

On the train to Wusong, I couldn't help but sigh to myself. Yūsuke Tsurumi said about summer travel: "The sun throws all the energy it has accumulated for hundreds of days onto the earth. In this bleak war between heaven and earth, mankind will certainly not shrink back in fear. Most people jump out of their own homes that they are tired of and rush into the arms of nature. This is travel." From this point of view, travelers in the hot summer seem close to warriors. In fact, for example, this trip to Wusong, I only feel that it is an outright theft of leisure, and there is no sense of competing with nature. If we really regard hiking under the hot sun as brave, then can we say that those who stay by the machines and boilers all day long are cowards? Mr. Tsurumi's words are correct, but this is only suitable for preaching to the fat people who "sleep well on hot summer days."

Travel is entertainment. Especially in summer, this entertainment should be extended to all people. Although at this moment, it can only be regarded as a dream, it will eventually be realized in the future.

Reading While Sweating 226

— Chen Zizhan

"Reading books while sweating incessantly, people all wonder what I seek. Do I seek further glory and advancement? I merely pass the long days to dispel my sorrow."

This is one of the poems called "Ningpu Book Affairs" written by Qin Guan of the Northern Song Dynasty, probably when he was demoted and exiled to Hengzhou because of a party scandal. Otherwise, the taste of complaint may not have been so strong. If he was a successful and wealthy man, he could spend his hot days "in pavilions by the water, savoring plums and floating melons." If he was a noble recluse who did not offend others or contend with the world, he could "lie under a north-facing window, with cool breezes blowing from time to time, considering himself a man from the time of Emperor Xi," comfortably escaping these hot May and June days. Helplessly, his fate destined him to fall into the stratum of scholar-officials, but he could not enjoy the blessings that scholar-officials could enjoy, but instead had to bear the burdens that scholar-officials were unwilling to bear. In that scorching summer, the days were too long, so he had to read books while sweating to dispel his worries and boredom!

These past few days, the weather in Shanghai has been particularly hot, and I really can't stand it. Reading books while sweating, why? I can't answer it myself. Remembering Qin Guan's poem, I can't help but feel moved.

Originally, such hot weather is most unsuitable for reading. You can go to the movie theater with air conditioning, or you can talk in a coffee shop with an electric fan, or you can go to the dance hall with summer resort facilities. Of course, ice cream, iced soda, and fruits are indispensable. Otherwise, you would be letting down this modern urban civilization. However, if you are tired of living in such a city, you will also think of the mountains and countryside, especially in this hot summer. Therefore, places such as Lushan, Moganshan, Huangshan, and Jigongshan have become "holy places" for civilized people in the city, high-class Chinese, and foreign gentlemen to escape the summer heat.

As for the vast majority of people who are not fortunate enough to go to such holy places to escape the heat, and cannot live in the city, and cannot enjoy the scientific civilization of summer resorts, they deserve it. If they are lucky enough to be literate, reading books to escape the summer heat is a good way, especially for those who have worries, they can use it to dispel their worries!

Naturally, this time is not the season for reading. Aren't all kinds of schools on summer vacation? However, reading books while sweating is ultimately different from hoeing weeds and planting vegetables. It can be seen that under the same "high sun," some people enjoy blessings because of it, while others see more hardship because of it. Only we bookworms, reading books while sweating, have joy in hardship and hardship in joy. It is still an ideal life of balanced happiness and hardship.

Sweat is not something to be cursed. If a person does not sweat when they should, they are sick, and aspirin, ephedra, and cinnamon twigs become holy medicines. If the sweat pores are blocked, like a blocked nose, breathing is not smooth, which is uncomfortable. If sweat cannot be secreted, like urine cannot be discharged, it is also impossible to survive. A little sweat is not a big sacrifice. Young masters and misses, old masters and ladies, don't be afraid. The average literati cannot carry on their shoulders or lift with their hands, and have very few opportunities for labor, so they don't sacrifice much sweat either. Not to mention sweating and suffering, on such a hot day, you sweat when you read books, and you sweat even when you don't read books. Moreover, "reading books does not forget to save the country, saving the country does not forget to read books," and reading books has "unexpected effects." Sweating your own sweat, reading your own books, and saving your own country, why not do it?

If young masters and misses issue declarations and shout slogans against my theory of reading books while sweating, I will not insist on my original views to achieve thoroughness. I am clear about this kind of worldliness. This confused article is too timid, so I will quote a poem that is said to be from a naughty child who ran away from school as the end of the talk.

"Spring is not a day for reading, hot summer days are good for sleeping. Autumn has mosquitoes and winter has snow, focus on preparing for next year."

Praying for Rain 228

I Come From the East (3) 229

— Xingye

Arriving Again in Chicago

On the map, the United States is a country about the same size as China. In fact, the prosperity of the United States is mostly concentrated on a straight line from New York to Chicago. Within these hundreds of miles, there are many large cities, large mines, and large factories that form the lifeline of American industry. Airplanes fly back and forth in the sky all day long, and telephones and telegrams are busy. Dozens of railways, like a bundle of large iron cables, tightly connect this large industrial area. In this transportation network, everything is fast, busy, passionate, and noisy.

After a night's ride in a large car, I, who was used to being mixed in with busyness and speed, actually felt quite tired. Especially when the car passed through the towering mountains and headed towards the coal-blackened city of Pittsburgh (Pittsburgh).

Pittsburgh—the hometown of countless great industrialists and great capitalists in the United States, is, in my opinion, the ugliest and dirtiest city in the world. Gray houses are built upside down on mountains with no green grass. The streets are so narrow, and the pedestrians on the road, regardless of gender, all have a cannibalistic look. Large red advertisements are painted on the walls and windows, like fresh blood left on the mouth of a poisonous snake.

In the mountains, thousands of chimneys spew out smoky coal smoke. In that hellish factory, how many Americans are selling their sweat and blood? Sweat and blood have formed the tens of millions of fortunes of steel tycoons and lead tycoons. Pittsburgh's steel and lead built New York's Wall Street, and above New York's Wall Street floats a so-called Washington government. Old Mellon, who served as the Minister of Finance for three dynasties, is the proud son of Pittsburgh. Carnegie, who once manipulated the fate of industries on both continents of Europe and America, came from Pittsburgh's steel shop as an apprentice. After Carnegie's steel company was sold to the bank tycoon Morgan, that tyrant of New York banking used his United States Steel Corporation to manipulate the fate of American and even world industries.

It was not easy to leave Pittsburgh's coal smoke. The car sped westward at a speed of five miles per hour. Large cities are strung together like beads to form this wonderful chain of capitalist countries. On this side is the automobile city cast by the money of Henry Ford; on the other side is the city of Akron, the center of the rubber industry. Cities like Clair and Layton gather tens of millions of workers, who are creating either a good or a bad future for the United States. New industrial cities have stretched out like mushrooms in the past fifty years. Among these many star-like cities, Chicago's position seems to be the bright moon that leads the group.

Education News

Ministry of Education Instructs Colleges and Above 230

Key Points for Improvement in Various Schools (4)

Tianjin Beiyang Institute of Technology 231

The college strictly enforces the full-time system for faculty and staff. The main faculty members are rich in teaching experience, and they are able to work hard in research while teaching many courses. Various examinations are also conducted seriously, which is a special advantage of the college. However, the following points still need to be improved in order to be practical and develop specialties.

(1) The equipment for the civil engineering and mechanical engineering departments and the basic physical experiment equipment for each department are not sufficient for application. Books and magazines are also lacking. Funds should be saved to add them year by year.

(2) The Department of Electrical Engineering and the Department of Architectural Engineering were approved to be added before. Now, it is found that most of the equipment for the Department of Electrical Engineering has not been purchased, and the Department of Architectural Engineering has no preparations. It is appropriate to postpone the opening of the Architectural Engineering Department. The Department of Electrical Engineering currently has only one grade and is taught in the same class as the Department of Mechanical Engineering. The original students can be merged into the Department of Mechanical Engineering. The college should carefully consider and submit it for approval. The Department of Chemical Engineering should be postponed. The Department of Aircraft Engineering should properly formulate establishment methods when equipment costs are secured and submit them to the Ministry for approval. Before the equipment funds are secured, courses and lectures such as aeronautics can be set up in the existing departments.

(3) The book lending system and student travel and visit fees should be gradually cancelled to transfer these funds to expand equipment. How to handle it can be submitted by the college for detailed opinions and properly formulated remedial measures for review and handling. It is also found that the books left by the former Department of Law of the college have many important works on law. It is a pity that they are not used. They can be handed over to the School of Law of National Peking University for safekeeping and utilization. You should consult with the university for handling.

Tianjin Private Institute of Industry and Commerce 232

The school's foundation and equipment are still based, and efforts should be made to improve other aspects. The key points that should be improved are presented below.

(1) The two colleges of industry and commerce of the college should be changed to science and engineering, business departments, mechanical and general business departments should be temporarily postponed.

(2) Curriculum standards and descriptions should be drafted as soon as possible and submitted to the Ministry for review and approval. Add two subjects of Party theory and Chinese and improve the content of teaching materials and focus on the study of practical problems in the country.

(3) Various material testing equipment and professional magazines should be purchased, and business practice equipment should also be added.

(4) The faculty and staff should be rehired and more people with teaching and school running experience should be hired. It should also be based on the principle of full-time.

(5) The school's academic atmosphere is very quiet, and teaching methods should be improved and the spirit of students' automatic research should be cultivated.

(6) The school's "Bachelor's Diploma" and "Class B Diploma" do not conform to the Ministry's regulations and should be cancelled. Other rules and regulations and organizational structures should be revised separately in accordance with current education laws and regulations and sent to the Ministry for review.

Hebei Women's Normal College 233

The administrative departments of the college can proceed in an orderly manner, the staff are dedicated to service, the students are diligent and simple, and the discipline is good. However, the following shortcomings still need to be strictly improved.

(1) The college has too many departments. It is difficult to achieve effective results by running with existing funds and teachers. It should be reduced appropriately to enrich it.

1. The two departments of English Education will stop enrollment from the summer vacation of this year and end year by year. However, teaching positions should still be established and taught seriously for English education subjects.

2. The three departments of Home Economics, Physical Education, and Music and Art should be changed to three specialized courses of Home Economics, Physical Education, and Art.

3. The number of students enrolled in the two departments of Chinese and History and Geography and the above three specialized courses should not exceed 80 each year. In the first year, attention must be paid to the training of basic subjects.

(2) The college's teachers' qualifications and experience are mostly unqualified. Full-time teachers are few in number and still hold positions outside the college. Among them, 12 people come from Peiping to teach in the college, which is inappropriate. (3) The college's past enrollment was not strict, and the students' level was mostly low. In the future, enrollment examinations should be conducted strictly, and students in the college should be trained seriously.

Explanation from the Ministry of Education

Qualification Criteria for Primary School Teachers 240

The Ministry of Education, based on a report from the Hunan Provincial Department of Education regarding doubts about the qualification of primary school teachers submitted by the Hengyang Education Bureau, requested instructions. The Ministry of Education instructed the department that, according to the Provisional Regulations for Rural Normal Schools revised in the province in the 20th year of the Republic [1931], the duration of study for rural normal schools that enroll junior high school graduates is two years, for primary school teachers who have the equivalent of junior high school education and have been engaged in education for more than one year, the duration of study is three years, and for those who enroll senior primary school graduates, the duration of study is four years. Graduates of rural normal schools in the province who meet the qualifications of the first item of the above regulations should be equivalent to graduates of the old-system normal schools. Those who meet the qualifications of the second item should be equivalent to graduates of the senior high school normal department. Those who meet the qualifications of the third item should be equivalent to graduates of simple rural normal schools. According to the report, before the promulgation of the Provisional Regulations for Rural Normal Schools, the duration of study at various rural normal schools was relatively shorter than the above regulations. The department did not state the admission qualifications of the graduates of various rural normal schools, and the ministry could not verify their qualifications. For the sake of appointment, the department should handle the admission qualifications and duration of study of graduates of various rural normal schools separately according to the provisions of Articles 78 and 79 of the primary school regulations.

Establishing Unified Revenue and Expenditure Measures 245

The Municipal Education Bureau yesterday ordered all municipal schools to be informed. The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau yesterday issued an order to all municipal schools stating that, according to the Municipal Government Order No. 10138, "Regarding the revenue, expenditure, deposit, and transfer of all funds of municipal schools, the Municipal Government has previously established unified revenue and expenditure measures, which should be managed uniformly by the Municipal Bank and ordered to be followed. It is now found that some schools in the urban area still deposit educational funds, educational funds, etc. in other banks, and have failed to comply with the order, which greatly hinders the unified revenue and expenditure in the future. We hereby request that you submit this to the mayor and order the Education Bureau to order all schools to comply with the previous order in the future regarding the revenue and expenditure of school funds, school building funds, and all educational funds, and to have them managed uniformly by this bank in order to comply with the law," etc. According to this, all funds received by various agencies, regardless of the item, should be submitted to the Municipal Bank and deposited into the Municipal Treasury account. This has been clearly stipulated in the unified revenue and expenditure measures and has been ordered to be followed. However, it is now the case that some schools in the urban area still deposit educational funds, educational funds, etc. in other banks, which is a violation of the law. The bureau has the responsibility to supervise and should immediately order the schools in the urban area to comply with the regulations on unified measures in the future regarding all educational funds, to send them to the Municipal Bank for handling at any time, and to pay attention to investigation. If the above-mentioned malpractices are found, they should be ordered to be changed and should not be neglected. In addition to ordering the office to reply, the bureau should follow and report this order. According to this, all schools should comply with the unified revenue and expenditure measures established by the Municipal Government regarding the receipt and payment of funds in the future and submit them to the Shanghai Municipal Bank for handling. They should also submit them to the bureau on a regular basis for forwarding, as before, and should not violate this order.

New Tennis Techniques (9) J. P.A+RMLYPARET, original author, Qian Yiqin and Hong Jun, joint translators

Copyright Reserved, Reproduction Prohibited 265

Chapter 4: The Right-Handed Forehand Stroke

Analysis of the most important stroke in tennis and explanation of the differences between various hitting methods 266

When returning the opponent's ball, Ground-Strokes, or hitting the ball after it bounces, should account for 80% of the time. Volleys, hitting the ball before it bounces, are rare. There are two types of strokes for handling ground balls: first, the forehand stroke, which is when the ball bounces to the player's right when facing the net (specifically for right-handed players; it's the opposite for left-handed players); second, the backhand stroke, which is when the ball bounces to the player's left when facing the net.

The forehand ground stroke is used very frequently, so it is a fundamental technique. Usually, experienced players will use this method to return the ball whenever possible, and they all consider it the easiest and most natural method.

When hitting a forehand, the player's right shoulder is behind the incoming ball, so the right hand has great striking power when it sweeps forward. However, when hitting a backhand, the player's right shoulder must be slightly in front of the incoming ball. At this time, the hitting action is inevitably restricted by the elbow, making it less natural than the forehand. Some players specialize in the backhand, achieving the same effect as the forehand. Even fewer players have perfected the backhand, and they sometimes enjoy using that side to hit the ball.

When hitting a forehand, it is very natural to twist the wrist forward. Conversely, when hitting a backhand, the wrist must be twisted backward, bending the knuckles forward. If the angle between the racket and the incoming ball is not accurate, the wrist will have difficulty being locked. Therefore, wrist movement is much freer in the forehand than in the backhand. Some players don't even twist their wrists when hitting a backhand; they simply handle it stiffly.

When moving forward to meet the incoming ball, the player must choose the direction of their stroke. After deciding on the direction, quickly move the feet according to the forehand or backhand stance, stepping on the left or right side of the ball. As for how to choose the direction of the stroke, it depends entirely on the player's position on the court and the opponent's position. If the incoming ball lands near the center of the court, it is very easy to decide the direction of the stroke, and in this situation, the forehand is used nine times out of ten. If the incoming ball is far from the body, it is impossible for the player to choose the direction of the stroke, so they have to assess the situation and deal with the crisis accordingly.
